
-----title
福州 (出生地)
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='da5b2f64c6844f7987a97c2fa2ce3388_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("da5b2f64c6844f7987a97c2fa2ce3388");'><span id='da5b2f64c6844f7987a97c2fa2ce3388_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=840&endYear=840')">840年</a>　约生于本年。居家乡福州侯官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=841&endYear=858')">841-858年</a>　居家乡侯官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='a1eea1621af14cc097125743c83177f6_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("a1eea1621af14cc097125743c83177f6");'><span id='a1eea1621af14cc097125743c83177f6_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=898&endYear=898')">898年</a>，59岁</div><div id='a1eea1621af14cc097125743c83177f6' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=898&endYear=898')">898年</a>　赴长安求职，过福州，别王审知。作品：《辞相府》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_47485' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47485' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47485?labeling=true' target='_blank'>辞相府<span class='inlineComment2'>（时蒙堂贴追赴阙）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（898年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47485")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47485_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_47485'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6976, "poem_allusion_47485")'>秦客</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_47485_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47485'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47485'>从汉至唐分五州，谁为将相作诸侯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47485'>闽江似镜正堪恋，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(6976, "poem_sentence_1_47485")'>秦客</span>如蓬难久留。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47485'>匹马忍辞藩屏去，小才宁副庙堂求。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47485'>今朝拜别<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_47485", 47485, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>幡幢</span>下，双泪如珠滴不休。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47485_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47485'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47485_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='9cf493555790471ebba5fb95eff71536_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9cf493555790471ebba5fb95eff71536");'><span id='9cf493555790471ebba5fb95eff71536_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=901&endYear=901')">901年</a>，62岁</div><div id='9cf493555790471ebba5fb95eff71536' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=901&endYear=901')">901年</a>　以监察御史里行充王审知武威军节度推官。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='7bfcb53e247541bc8af5783b4044d5b5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7bfcb53e247541bc8af5783b4044d5b5");'><span id='7bfcb53e247541bc8af5783b4044d5b5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=908')">902-908年</a>，63-69岁</div><div id='7bfcb53e247541bc8af5783b4044d5b5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年</a>　受命为开元寺灵山塑北方毗沙门天王碑撰碑记。作品：《灵山塑北方毗沙门天王碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>灵山塑北方毗沙门天王碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（902年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376596")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376596'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376596'>列藩之业有地。有地之职有民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376596_comment'></div>有民之道。兴礼乐敦忠孝以行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376596_comment'></div>然后谋谋者也。筑城池居其一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376596_comment'></div>城既筑。进道德以居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376596_comment'></div>树神祗以尸之。为一方之巨防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376596_comment'></div>虽永古而无疑。我相府琅琊王王公之有闽越也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376596_comment'></div>具列藩之业。修有地之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376596_comment'></div>行有民之道。自乾宁四年丁巳至天祐二年壬戌凡六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376596_comment'></div>礼乐兴。忠孝敦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376596_comment'></div>乃谋及城池。城池既谋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376596_comment'></div>乃尸及神祗。于是于开元寺之灵山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376596_comment'></div>塑北方毗沙门天王<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>一铺</span>。全部落已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376596_comment'></div>镇于城焉。大矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376596_comment'></div>所谓阐六韬。浚七德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376596_comment'></div>建<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/28/Comments/0")'>阳功</span>。配阴骘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376596_comment'></div>夫毗沙门<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>梵音</span>。唐言多闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376596_comment'></div>始自于阗刹利之英奇。膺世尊帝释之锡号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376596_comment'></div>居须弥山北。住水晶宫殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376596_comment'></div>领药义众为帝释外臣。以护南赡部洲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376596_comment'></div>其道入大乘。得无生法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376596_comment'></div>忍住闻声。證不还果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376596_comment'></div>谨稽我公之筑城也。恢守地养民之本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376596_comment'></div>隆暂劳永逸之策。其名举一而生三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376596_comment'></div>法阳数也。曰大城焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376596_comment'></div>南月城焉。北月城焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376596_comment'></div>周圆二十六里四千八百丈。基凿于地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376596_comment'></div>十有五尺。杵土胎石而上<span class='inlineComment2'>（上声）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376596_comment'></div>上高二十尺。厚十有七尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376596_comment'></div>外甃以砖。凡一千五百万片。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376596_comment'></div>上架以屋。其屋曰廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376596_comment'></div>其大城之廊也。一千八百有十间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376596_comment'></div>自廊凸而出之为敌楼。楼之层者二十有三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376596_comment'></div>又角立之楼六。其二者层复层焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376596_comment'></div>皆栏干钩联。参差焕赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376596_comment'></div>而廊之若干步<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>一铺</span>。铺各一鼓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376596_comment'></div>而司更焉。凡三十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376596_comment'></div>谓之更铺。其四面之门八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376596_comment'></div>其南曰福安门。福安之东曰清平门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376596_comment'></div>西曰清远门。其北曰安善门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376596_comment'></div>安善门之东曰通远门。其东曰通津门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376596_comment'></div>通津之北曰济川门。其西曰善化门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376596_comment'></div>皆铁扇铜扃。开阳阖阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376596_comment'></div>门之上仍揭以楼。三间两挟两噏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376596_comment'></div>修廊双面远碧。门之左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376596_comment'></div>又引而出之。为之亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376596_comment'></div>两间一厦。又匪楼之门九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376596_comment'></div>曰暗门焉。又水门三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376596_comment'></div>其二树棂筛波。卸帆入舟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376596_comment'></div>鸣舷柳浦。回环一郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376596_comment'></div>堤诸万户。注之以堰二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376596_comment'></div>渡之以桥九。镜莹虹横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376596_comment'></div>交舫走蹄。斯大城之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376596_comment'></div>粤南月城也。东贮九仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376596_comment'></div>西盛乌石之二山。嘉树蓄云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376596_comment'></div>茂草藏兽。城上之廊一千十有三间<span class='inlineComment2'>（其中七间谓之徘徊）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376596_comment'></div>敌楼四十有九。楼之层者三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376596_comment'></div>其门二。曰登庸门<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>道清门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376596_comment'></div>其上之楼。其下之扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376596_comment'></div>左右之引亭。建暗门八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376596_comment'></div>水门二。其堰一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376596_comment'></div>其桥五。及廊之更铺二十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376596_comment'></div>悉与大城类。其外之东西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376596_comment'></div>复距而出之。谓之横城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376596_comment'></div>其东也。城上之廊四十二间五厦<span class='inlineComment2'>（其中二间是两面之敌楼）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376596_comment'></div>其门一。斯南月城之制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376596_comment'></div>伊北月城也。城上之廊六百四十二间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376596_comment'></div>敌楼二十有六。楼之层者十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376596_comment'></div>其门二。曰道泰门严胜门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376596_comment'></div>其上之楼。其下之扉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376596_comment'></div>左右之引亭。建暗门四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376596_comment'></div>水门二。其桥一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376596_comment'></div>及廊之更铺十有四。复与南月城类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376596_comment'></div>又觜而出之。谓之横城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376596_comment'></div>城上之廊五间一厦。其门一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376596_comment'></div>斯北月城之制也。其东画长川以为洫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376596_comment'></div>西连乎南<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>。盘别浦以为沟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376596_comment'></div>悉通海䲡朝夕盈缩之波。底泽鳞介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376596_comment'></div>岸泊艓艛。北截越王之故山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376596_comment'></div>派西湖以为隍。若鳌之负。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376596_comment'></div>如瓯之置。轩轩然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376596_comment'></div>翼翼然。真谓天设之府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376596_comment'></div>神开之地也。既而我公一旦膝分席校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376596_comment'></div>鳞军堵耋。陈大会以落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376596_comment'></div>而言曰。惟闽越之为藩屏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376596_comment'></div>建汀二疆束其右。岩千而壑万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376596_comment'></div>溟海巨流濒其左。涛雷而浪霆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376596_comment'></div>信乎江山奇险。无以加之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376596_comment'></div>矧今新之以城壁。城壁之以铁石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376596_comment'></div>古人言得地。又言守地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376596_comment'></div>又言坚壁。岂不以得地而居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376596_comment'></div>守地以城。城以坚壁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376596_comment'></div>信不疑矣。然则吾之戴恩忝土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376596_comment'></div>勤勤恳恳。不以江山奇险之为奇险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376596_comment'></div>不以城壁铁石之为铁石也。修道德树神祇以居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376596_comment'></div>毗沙门之天王。自天宝中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376596_comment'></div>使于阗者得其真还。愈增宇内之敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376596_comment'></div>旋大夫芮国公荆渚之塑也。凡百城池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376596_comment'></div>莫不一之。斯旧城之北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376596_comment'></div>往规也<span class='inlineComment2'>（旧天王在子城北也）</span>。斯新城之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376596_comment'></div>今城也。且胜莫胜于开元寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376596_comment'></div>尚莫尚于寺之灵山。阜寺之艮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376596_comment'></div>控城之乙。祖僧六叶雁其下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376596_comment'></div>珉石一拳星其上<span class='inlineComment2'>（庐山湾落星石上有佛舍）</span>。剑池澈写。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376596_comment'></div>飞山奔揖。足以象水精而莹宫殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376596_comment'></div>掀庙貌以卫城池。爰将择工之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376596_comment'></div>搜塑之妙。制乎圣贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376596_comment'></div>俄然化出。身被金甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376596_comment'></div>手擎雁塔。地祇下捧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376596_comment'></div>天将前拥。光灼灼而如将动摇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376596_comment'></div>神雄雄而若欲<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/218/Comments/0")'>叱咤</span>。观之者皆谓须弥拔宅于是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376596_comment'></div>于阗分身于是矣。而复翼僧堂而右邃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376596_comment'></div>膊钟楼而左突。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_111_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/223/Comments/0")'>毳锡</span>百萃其夏午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376596_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/224/Comments/0")'>蒲鲸</span>六吼其宵加。信为尘间之北方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376596_comment'></div>连营之灵域也。讫命小从事滔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376596_comment'></div>刊贞石而碑之。滔不敢牢让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376596_comment'></div>斋戒三日。抽毫而书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376596_comment'></div>猗欤天王。因果则释氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376596_comment'></div>猛勇则兵权。启愿而愿从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376596_comment'></div>云战而战胜。至如挥额汗以为童子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376596_comment'></div>却修罗之师。擎手塔以贮弥陀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376596_comment'></div>解天鼓之赴。爰皆肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376596_comment'></div>克致感通。洎唐有土蕃之黩也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376596_comment'></div>豆面以行疹。仪金以现人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376596_comment'></div>啮戈以生鼠。与彼时之元应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376596_comment'></div>盖大同而小异。况迩则咸通季蛮之侵蜀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376596_comment'></div>蜀人亟祈。褐衣倏以乘空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376596_comment'></div>目光㸌以照地。蛇将奔穴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376596_comment'></div>龟竟全城。夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376596_comment'></div>则护南赡部洲。岂虚言哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376596_comment'></div>今我公之至诚通日月。宏愿质鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376596_comment'></div>以旷世之功业。托无生之法力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376596_comment'></div>岂昔时之有是。而今日之不然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376596_comment'></div>虽体苍苍而无言。因乃昭昭而有鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376596_comment'></div>辄为之铭。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376596_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_134_1376596'>受命帝释。封邑须弥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376596_comment'></div>金甲俨被。药义雄随。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376596_comment'></div>越七金山。突修罗师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376596_comment'></div>入大乘妙。与声闻差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376596_comment'></div>于阗分身。皇唐卫国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376596_comment'></div>若加善祷。咸蒙圣力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376596_comment'></div>雁塞烟尘。龟城戈戟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376596_comment'></div>虏骑犹东。蛮车未北。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376596_comment'></div>现以真仪。亡乎悖德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376596_comment'></div>懿彼闽越。大哉侯王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376596_comment'></div>仗钺务本。筑城为防。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376596_comment'></div>石取它山。壤堑联冈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376596_comment'></div>謺百厥雉。累千乎廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376596_comment'></div>却铁之触。疲羽之祥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376596_comment'></div>奔马辔并。驰车轨方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376596_comment'></div>巢凤于楼。蛰龙于隍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376596_comment'></div>如岳斯立。如翼斯张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376596_comment'></div>不有依凭。曷旌扃鐍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376596_comment'></div>台略俄启。神驱遽设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376596_comment'></div>铁须卓竖。漆瞳<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_153_1376596", 1376596, "Clauses/307/Comments/0")'>曝昳</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376596_comment'></div>捧足神俯。持剑将列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376596_comment'></div>月殿巍峨。灵山巀嶭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376596_comment'></div>法逮无生。权惟有兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376596_comment'></div>昔之若是。今肯忘情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376596_comment'></div>闽山永高。闽江永清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376596_comment'></div>厥宜识之。盘石斯城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376596_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_160_1376596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1376596'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_56_1376596_0'>⑴ 郭璞记南台江沙合即有宰相而我公膺期今登庸门外桥名沙合桥</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1376596_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年</a>　为王审知母撰祭文。作品：《祭钱塘秦国太夫人》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376611' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376611' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376611?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭钱塘秦国太夫人<span class='inlineComment2'>（代闽王）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（902年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376611")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376611_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376611'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376611'>维天复二年岁次壬戌。敬祭于故秦国太夫人之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376611_comment'></div>夫生帝王则若文母。方钟至圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376611_comment'></div>生人臣则若<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376611", 1376611, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>陶母</span>。方降大贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376611_comment'></div>信夫韬昴宿之耀于胸襟。掬嵩山之气为怀抱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376611_comment'></div>岂容易哉。伏惟明灵天资妇道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376611_comment'></div>神授母仪。金石不足喻其贞明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376611_comment'></div>芝兰不足表其芬馥。训逾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1376611", 1376611, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>孟织</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376611_comment'></div>智迈谢围。颜氏子则提育圣人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376611_comment'></div>曹大家则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376611", 1376611, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>师资</span>诸女。既作闺门之上瑞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376611_comment'></div>乃生英杰于皇家。立旷代之鸿勋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376611_comment'></div>拥两藩之龙节。食则万钱调膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376611_comment'></div>禄则三世及亲。见䌽衣则衣锦之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376611_comment'></div>见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376611", 1376611, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>冰鲤</span>则和羹之味。腾辉女史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376611_comment'></div>兴咏国风。推于古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376611_comment'></div>实无伦比。乃由懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376611_comment'></div>致此大荣。呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376611_comment'></div>灵药难求。流光易谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376611_comment'></div>本冀霜松而永寿。忽惊风烛以斯零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376611_comment'></div>竟成举世之悲伤。空切至诚之号慕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376611_comment'></div>审知幸攀令嗣。获忝亲邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376611_comment'></div>论交既契于金兰。抹泣乃同于亲属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376611_comment'></div>辄陈薄奠。用表悲诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376611_comment'></div>敢冀明灵。依稀歆鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376611_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1376611_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年7月</a>　为陈黯集撰序。作品：《颖川陈先生集序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376580' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376580' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376580?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍川陈先生集序</a><span class='authorDate'>（902年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376580")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376580_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376580'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376580'>唐设进士科垂三百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376580_comment'></div>有司之取士也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376580_comment'></div>喻之明镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376580_comment'></div>喻之平衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376580_comment'></div>未尝不以至公为之主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376580_comment'></div>而得丧之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376580_comment'></div>或失于明镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376580_comment'></div>或差于平衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376580_comment'></div>何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376580_comment'></div>俾其负不羁之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376580_comment'></div>蕴出人之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376580_comment'></div>殁身末路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376580_comment'></div>抱恨泉台者多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376580_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376580_comment'></div>岂天之否其至公之道邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376580_comment'></div>抑人之自坎其命邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376580_comment'></div>颍川陈先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376580_comment'></div>实斯人之谓与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376580_comment'></div>先生讳黯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376580_comment'></div>字希孺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376580_comment'></div>父讳贽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376580_comment'></div>通经及第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376580_comment'></div>娶江夏黄夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376580_comment'></div>贤而生先生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376580_comment'></div>无昆弟姊妹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376580_comment'></div>十岁能诗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376580_comment'></div>十三袖诗一通谒清源牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376580_comment'></div>其首篇咏歌河阳花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376580_comment'></div>向时豆新愈<span class='inlineComment2'>（疮之如豆）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376580_comment'></div>牧戏之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376580_comment'></div>藻才而花貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376580_comment'></div>胡不咏歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376580_comment'></div>先生应声曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376580_comment'></div>玳瑁应难比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376580_comment'></div>斑犀定不加。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376580_comment'></div>天嫌未端正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376580_comment'></div>满面与装花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376580_comment'></div>由是声名大振于州里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376580_comment'></div>十七为词赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376580_comment'></div>作苏武谒汉武帝陵庙赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376580_comment'></div>便为作者推伏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376580_comment'></div>二十为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376580_comment'></div>先生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1376580", 1376580, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>松姿柳态</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376580_comment'></div>山屹陂注。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376580_comment'></div>语默有程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376580_comment'></div>进退可法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376580_comment'></div>早孤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376580_comment'></div>事太夫人弥孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376580_comment'></div>熙熙愉愉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376580_comment'></div>承颜侍膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376580_comment'></div>虽隆云路之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376580_comment'></div>终确䌽衣之恋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376580_comment'></div>既而及其子蔚冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376580_comment'></div>太夫人勉之曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376580_comment'></div>付蔚于潘岳之筵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376580_comment'></div>俟尔于郤诜之桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376580_comment'></div>方起于乡荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376580_comment'></div>求试贡闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376580_comment'></div>己过不惑之年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376580_comment'></div>乃会昌乙丑逮咸通乙酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376580_comment'></div>其间以宁家兼在疚之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376580_comment'></div>断绝往来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376580_comment'></div>吴楚之江山辛勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376580_comment'></div>秦雍之槐蝉叹嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376580_comment'></div>知已之许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376580_comment'></div>与同郡<span class='inlineComment2'>（指泉州）</span>王肱萧枢同邑林颢漳浦赫连韬福州陈蔇陈发詹雄同时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376580_comment'></div>而名价相上下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376580_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376580_comment'></div>斯八贤皆以不羁之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376580_comment'></div>出人之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376580_comment'></div>恳恳乎进趋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376580_comment'></div>恂恂乎乡党。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376580_comment'></div>而无所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376580_comment'></div>岂天之竟否其至公邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376580_comment'></div>抑人之自坎其命邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376580_comment'></div>俾有司失其明镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376580_comment'></div>差其平衡之如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376580_comment'></div>结冤气于名路之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376580_comment'></div>衔汞恨于泉台之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376580_comment'></div>岂不甚与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376580_comment'></div>先生之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376580_comment'></div>词不尚奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376580_comment'></div>切于理也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376580_comment'></div>意不偶立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376580_comment'></div>重师古也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376580_comment'></div>其诗篇词赋檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376580_comment'></div>皆精而切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376580_comment'></div>故于官试尤工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376580_comment'></div>滔即先生之内侄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376580_comment'></div>自丱趋隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376580_comment'></div>洎随计之岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376580_comment'></div>先生下世后二十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376580_comment'></div>而忝登甲第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376580_comment'></div>东归之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376580_comment'></div>求遗藁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376580_comment'></div>其季子蘧泣曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376580_comment'></div>兵火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376580_comment'></div>少得其文三十一首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376580_comment'></div>赋若干首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376580_comment'></div>他处得诗若干首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376580_comment'></div>敬俟增而后述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376580_comment'></div>天复元年<span class='inlineComment2'>（辛酉）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376580_comment'></div>滔叨闵相之辟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376580_comment'></div>旋使钱塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376580_comment'></div>与罗郎中隐遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376580_comment'></div>隐曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376580_comment'></div>咸通初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376580_comment'></div>与先生定交于蒲津秋赋之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376580_comment'></div>赋则五老化为流星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376580_comment'></div>诗则汉武横汾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376580_comment'></div>先生之作也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376580_comment'></div>为试官严郎中下都之吟讽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376580_comment'></div>秋场五十人之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_112_1376580", 1376580, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>降仰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376580_comment'></div>今遗藁可丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376580_comment'></div>愿为之序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376580_comment'></div>既还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376580_comment'></div>不及求增。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376580_comment'></div>谨以所得之文赋诗笺檄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376580_comment'></div>分为五卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376580_comment'></div>收泪搦管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376580_comment'></div>为之前序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376580_comment'></div>将寓正郎为之后序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376580_comment'></div>正郎负宇内之雄名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376580_comment'></div>用释泉台之永恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376580_comment'></div>时天复二年秋七月十日也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_124_1376580_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=902&endYear=902')">902年7月</a>　请罗隐为陈黯集撰序。作品：《与罗隐郞中书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376548'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376548'>故表丈遗文。盛叙古人之重存殁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376548_comment'></div>爰捧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1376548", 1376548, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>诺金</span>。感涕之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376548_comment'></div>实刻肌骨。然以郎中十五兄相逢京辇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376548_comment'></div>得志金兰。虽备熟于行文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376548_comment'></div>恐未周于平昔。而滔以内外之戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376548_comment'></div>始终所详。敢以小才为之前叙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376548_comment'></div>诚以麟经下笔。诸生不合措辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376548_comment'></div>而马史抽毫。汉代还陈别录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376548_comment'></div>伏惟慈造。必践前言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376548_comment'></div>西望祷祈。可以鉴料。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376548_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1376548_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=903&endYear=903')">903年</a>　居王审知幕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=904&endYear=904')">904年</a>　唐遣右拾遗翁承赞加王审知检校太保，封琅琊王。黄滔赠以诗。作品：《辄吟七言四韵攀寄翁文尧拾遗》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《送翁拾遗》<span "黄滔", "poem_title_47466")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47466_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47466'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47466'>唐设高科表用文，吾曹谁作谏垣臣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47466'>甄山秀气旷千古，凤阙华恩钟二人。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47466'>起草便论天上事，如君不是世间身。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47466'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_47466", 47466, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>龙头</span>龙尾前年梦，今日须怜应若神<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47466'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_47466'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_47466_0'>⑴ 滔卯年冬在宛陵，梦文尧作状头及第。又申四月十二夜在清源，梦。到殿前，东道自西厉声唱，翁某拜右省拾遗</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_47466_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_47425' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47425' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47425?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送翁拾遗</a><span class='authorDate'>（904年）</span><span ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=904&endYear=904')">904年</a>　收封渭信，撰诗寄之。作品：《寄同年封舍人渭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_47447' class='_poem'><div id='poem_content_47445'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47445'>听尽莺声出雍州，秦吴烟月十经秋。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47445_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
