ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=905&endYear=905')">905年2月</a>　为莆山灵岩寺撰碑铭。作品：《莆山灵岩寺碑铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376598' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376598' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376598?labeling=true' target='_blank'>莆山灵岩寺碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（905年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376598")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376598_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376598'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376598'>释波东流。涌为花宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376598_comment'></div>花宫之构。咸宅灵秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376598_comment'></div>灵秀之启。其或神授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376598_comment'></div>则知融结之始。已有待于金圣人也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376598_comment'></div>粤灵岩寺。乃莆山之灵秀焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376598_comment'></div>神授焉。懿夫岳立大山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376598_comment'></div>堆下数峰。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>面乙</span>臂坤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376598_comment'></div>石嵌松瘦。昔梁陈间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376598_comment'></div>邑儒荥阳郑生家之。生严乎一堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376598_comment'></div>架以诗书。既而秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376598_comment'></div>一夕。风月清朗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376598_comment'></div>俄有神人。鹤发麻衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376598_comment'></div>丈馀其状。见于堂曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376598_comment'></div>诚易兹为佛宇。善莫大焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376598_comment'></div>生拜而诺。瞬而失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376598_comment'></div>旋以堂居僧像佛。献其居为金仙院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376598_comment'></div>即陈永定二年庚申也<span class='inlineComment2'>（鹤发麻衣西天之谓故号金仙）</span>。山水推其奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376598_comment'></div>鹤发增其异。缁锡日萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376598_comment'></div>院落日峻。隋开皇九年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376598_comment'></div>升为寺焉。左漱寒泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376598_comment'></div>右拥謺巘。危楼豁壶公之翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376598_comment'></div>上方视䲡海之波。唐景云二年辛亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376598_comment'></div>寺僧志彦入内。背文讲四分律。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376598_comment'></div>睿宗嘉之。锡号聪明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376598_comment'></div>彦因获言所居寺之自。复有僧无际持妙法莲华经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376598_comment'></div>感石上涌白泉。僧殁而泉变清焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376598_comment'></div>遂膺敕额为灵岩寺。太和二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376598_comment'></div>殿中彭城刘公轲幕提泉印。聆寺之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376598_comment'></div>不卸而宿。候吏不蔬而午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376598_comment'></div>掬泉而漱。随手以涸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376598_comment'></div>其石今坎于上方之上。其僧复有元悟元准慧全省文灵敞无了。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376598_comment'></div>悉间生祇园。坚持密行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376598_comment'></div>或临坛表德。或降虎示真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376598_comment'></div>厥众如云。厥施若市。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376598_comment'></div>洎武宗皇帝乙丑之否。邑之东有敬善寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376598_comment'></div>民井而居之。乾有玉涧寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376598_comment'></div>民亩而田之。独兹之奇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376598_comment'></div>豪人互以金输。为幽宅之卜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376598_comment'></div>若有之卫。竟不克遂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376598_comment'></div>敞公了公乃帽首绦腰。沉踪处晦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376598_comment'></div>逮宣宗皇帝之复。索之于石罅云根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376598_comment'></div>归之于芜基烧址。山灵之感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376598_comment'></div>行膻之慕。投金执斲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376598_comment'></div>匪招匪劝。不越闰而其宇<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>鳞鳞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376598_comment'></div>其徒翼翼。敞公咸通六年秋八月云灭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376598_comment'></div>靡风而大树折庭。靡触而大殿倾瓦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376598_comment'></div>了公八年冬十月<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>坐亡</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>色身</span>不坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376598_comment'></div>今龟阳之号真身大师者也。则知僧以行而神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376598_comment'></div>其亦地以灵而感。若乃轩轩月殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376598_comment'></div>蔼蔼松门。醍醐雨天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376598_comment'></div>琉璃镜地。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>慧烛</span>九枝而吐燄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376598_comment'></div>慈云五色以垂阴。推于瓯越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376598_comment'></div>居之甲乙。今仆射琅琊王公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376598_comment'></div>牧民之外。雅隆净土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376598_comment'></div>论及灵胜。以为东山神泉之比<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376598_comment'></div>缮经五千卷。于兹华创藏而藏<span class='inlineComment2'>（平声）</span>焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376598_comment'></div>即天祐二年春二月也。初侍御史济南林公藻与其季水部员外郎蕴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376598_comment'></div>贞元中谷兹而业文。欧阳四门舍泉山而诣焉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376598_comment'></div>其后皆中殊科。御史省试珠还合浦赋有神授之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376598_comment'></div>水部应贤良方正科擅比干之誉<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。欧阳垂四门之号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376598_comment'></div>与韩文公齐名。得非山水之灵秀乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376598_comment'></div>元和才子章孝标邵楚苌朱可名寄诗以题。大中中<span class='inlineComment2'>（宣宗元年丁卯号大中凡十三年）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376598_comment'></div>颍川陈蔚江夏黄楷长沙欧阳碣兼愚慕三贤之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_62_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/124/Comments/0")'>懿躅</span>。葺斋于东峰十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376598_comment'></div>咸通乾符之际<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。豪贵塞龙门之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376598_comment'></div>平人艺士。十攻九败。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376598_comment'></div>故颍川之以家冤也与。二三子率不西迈而遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376598_comment'></div>奋然凡二十四年。于举场幸忝甲第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376598_comment'></div>东归之寻旧址。苍苔四謺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376598_comment'></div>嘉树双亚<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑸</sup>。访旧僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376598_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_69_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/138/Comments/0")'>云扃</span>十扣。雪顶一存。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376598_comment'></div>于是谨祝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_70_1376598", 1376598, "Clauses/140/Comments/0")'>金仪</span>。益誓邱祷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376598_comment'></div>以谢兹山之灵秀。刻铭贞石。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376598_comment'></div>兼补前贤之未述。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376598_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_73_1376598'>山奇孕神。地胜惟灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376598_comment'></div>萤窗既夜。鹤发斯形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376598_comment'></div>一亩请宫。双莲建扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376598_comment'></div>洞深夏寒。林茂冬青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376598_comment'></div>松竹铿乐。峰峦豁屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376598_comment'></div>皛迷蟾窟。茫眺䲡溟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376598_comment'></div>持经僧志。涌石泉泠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376598_comment'></div>四分律讲。万乘君听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376598_comment'></div>敕飞额降。寺以灵名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376598_comment'></div>不有地祥。焉动天庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376598_comment'></div>大士鸿生。珠明桂馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376598_comment'></div>良牧耸闻。华构藏经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376598_comment'></div>浩劫不泯。匪兹曷丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376598_comment'></div>敬祝巉岩。勒石以铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376598_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_87_1376598_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1376598'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_54_1376598_0'>⑴ 神泉寺在府城之东山其泉亦自僧感而涌也</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_57_1376598_0'>⑵ 四门家晋江泉山在郡城之北其集有与王式书云莆阳读书即兹寺也</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_59_1376598_0'>⑶ 策云臣远祖比干因谏而死天不厌直生微臣也</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_63_1376598_0'>⑷ 懿宗元年庚辰改咸通凡十四年僖宗元年甲午改乾符</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_68_1376598_0'>⑸ 今东峰双龙眼树即往岁书斋之庭阴也</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1376598_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=905&endYear=905')">905年4月</a>　受命为大唐福州报恩寺定光多宝塔撰碑记。作品：《大唐福州报恩寺定光多宝塔碑记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376595' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376595' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376595?labeling=true' target='_blank'>大唐福州报恩定光多宝塔碑记</a><span class='authorDate'>（905年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376595")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376595_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376595'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376595'>金圣人之教功与德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376595_comment'></div>鲁圣人之教忠与孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376595_comment'></div>以忠孝之祈功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376595_comment'></div>莫之大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376595_comment'></div>天复元年辛酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376595_comment'></div>天子西巡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376595_comment'></div>岐汴交兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376595_comment'></div>京洛禺禺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376595_comment'></div>我威武军节度使相府琅琊王王公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376595_comment'></div>祀天地鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376595_comment'></div>以至忠之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376595_comment'></div>发大誓愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376595_comment'></div>于开元之寺造塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376595_comment'></div>建号寿山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376595_comment'></div>仍辅以经藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376595_comment'></div>乞车驾之还宫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376595_comment'></div>其三年甲子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376595_comment'></div>以大孝之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376595_comment'></div>发大誓愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376595_comment'></div>于兹九仙山造塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376595_comment'></div>建号定光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376595_comment'></div>仍辅以经藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376595_comment'></div>为先君司空先秦国太夫人元昆故司空荐祉于幽阴也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376595_comment'></div>大矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376595_comment'></div>赫赫忠诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376595_comment'></div>恳恳孝思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376595_comment'></div>以国以家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376595_comment'></div>以明以幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376595_comment'></div>胡天地之不动欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376595_comment'></div>胡鬼神之不感欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376595_comment'></div>释之西天谓之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>窣堵波</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376595_comment'></div>中华谓之塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376595_comment'></div>塔制以层。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376595_comment'></div>增其敬也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376595_comment'></div>造之获无量无边功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376595_comment'></div>初我公以宏才妙略之有藩维。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376595_comment'></div>以仁智神鉴之谋远大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376595_comment'></div>谓闽越之江山奇秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376595_comment'></div>土风深厚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376595_comment'></div>而府城坐龙之腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376595_comment'></div>乌石九仙二山耸龙之角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376595_comment'></div>屹屹岩岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376595_comment'></div>孱孱<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>颜颜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376595_comment'></div>两排地面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376595_comment'></div>双立空际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376595_comment'></div>怪石如墉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376595_comment'></div>回冈如揖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376595_comment'></div>东衔沧海以镜豁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376595_comment'></div>西走建溪而带萦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376595_comment'></div>气色<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/49/Comments/0")'>蒙茸</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376595_comment'></div>风云蓬勃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376595_comment'></div>非仙宫佛寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376595_comment'></div>不可以乘龙之角。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376595_comment'></div>大龙之腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376595_comment'></div>何乌石二而九仙旷<span class='inlineComment2'>（乌石山有神光天王二寺）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376595_comment'></div>岂非代虚其作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376595_comment'></div>地秘其期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376595_comment'></div>以待我公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376595_comment'></div>况古仙鍊骨之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376595_comment'></div>升真之迹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376595_comment'></div>一旦之新城月圆<span class='inlineComment2'>（壬戌岁我公卜筑其外城号月城）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376595_comment'></div>二山之嘉气云连。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376595_comment'></div>森上介。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376595_comment'></div>掀大旆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376595_comment'></div>或旬或朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376595_comment'></div>眷于粉堞之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376595_comment'></div>时行时止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376595_comment'></div>卜于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>烟峦</span>之堀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376595_comment'></div>得峻中之平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376595_comment'></div>平中之峻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376595_comment'></div>凸而不隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376595_comment'></div>凹而不卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376595_comment'></div>树翳荟以奇姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376595_comment'></div>草芊眠而别翠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376595_comment'></div>遂从宏愿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376595_comment'></div>启兹塔之基焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376595_comment'></div>塔之科也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376595_comment'></div>恐山之偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376595_comment'></div>忧地之入。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376595_comment'></div>将堑平壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376595_comment'></div>五十尺之深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376595_comment'></div>百有馀尺之阔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_82_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/82/Comments/1")'>杵土</span>积石而上<span class='inlineComment2'>（上声）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376595_comment'></div>逮二十尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376595_comment'></div>瞥然虹见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376595_comment'></div>莹然穴贮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376595_comment'></div>俄以珠宝之获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376595_comment'></div>坐以金钱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376595_comment'></div>大不及拳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376595_comment'></div>光能夺目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376595_comment'></div>于时清风四来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376595_comment'></div>海天扩开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376595_comment'></div>烟霞蓊蔚于城隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>鸾鹤</span>盘旋于林表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376595_comment'></div>举闽之军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376595_comment'></div>倾闽之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376595_comment'></div>以趋以走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376595_comment'></div>以歌以咏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376595_comment'></div>既而畚锸投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376595_comment'></div>般倕奋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376595_comment'></div>内甃以砖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376595_comment'></div>凡四十万口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376595_comment'></div>外沟以木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376595_comment'></div>盖百其巧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376595_comment'></div>七层八面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376595_comment'></div>玲珑䆗窱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376595_comment'></div>榱桷栏楯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376595_comment'></div>轇轕𭩚枒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376595_comment'></div>云楣翼环。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/109/Comments/0")'>圭斗</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_109_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/109/Comments/1")'>鳞蹙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376595_comment'></div>雕锼丹雘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376595_comment'></div>曲尽其妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376595_comment'></div>方七十有七尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376595_comment'></div>高二百尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376595_comment'></div>相轮之四十尺参之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376595_comment'></div>悬轮之铎一百九十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376595_comment'></div>悬层之铎五十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376595_comment'></div>角瓦之神五十有六。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376595_comment'></div>其内也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376595_comment'></div>则门门面面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376595_comment'></div>缋以金像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376595_comment'></div>不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376595_comment'></div>登之者若身在梵天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376595_comment'></div>瞻之者觉神离赡部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376595_comment'></div>嶪嶪然触圆青而直上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376595_comment'></div>野鹤经之而高翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376595_comment'></div>疑掠其腹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376595_comment'></div>鳞鳞然压峭碧而崛起。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376595_comment'></div>地祇感之而下捧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376595_comment'></div>疑殚其力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376595_comment'></div>其相轮也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376595_comment'></div>我公誓愿之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376595_comment'></div>仲氏司徒自清源闻而感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376595_comment'></div>铸而资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376595_comment'></div>虽从人力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376595_comment'></div>悉类<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_135_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/135/Comments/0")'>神功</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376595_comment'></div>谨按妙法莲花品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376595_comment'></div>自地涌塔于佛之前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376595_comment'></div>其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_138_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/138/Comments/0")'>幢幡</span>璎珞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376595_comment'></div>玛瑙车渠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376595_comment'></div>七盘四悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376595_comment'></div>乘虚耀日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376595_comment'></div>乃多宝之佛发大誓愿之感现也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376595_comment'></div>繇是以斯塔取如来之嘉号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376595_comment'></div>号之曰定光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376595_comment'></div>以其感珠之现。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376595_comment'></div>眸于自地之涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376595_comment'></div>故联之于多宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376595_comment'></div>本于孝思荐劬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376595_comment'></div>故冠之以报恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376595_comment'></div>此其义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376595_comment'></div>夫如是大雄之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_152_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>出死入生</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376595_comment'></div>至诚之神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376595_comment'></div>感天动地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376595_comment'></div>若乃沉沉夜壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376595_comment'></div>浩浩世尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376595_comment'></div>莫不以兹元符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376595_comment'></div>承彼慧日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376595_comment'></div>超于三千大千之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376595_comment'></div>游乎<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_160_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/160/Comments/0")'>二十八天</span>者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1376595_comment'></div>苟不之然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1376595_comment'></div>则凡彼经文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1376595_comment'></div>悉为之虚语耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1376595_comment'></div>又焉能垂信于百千年之后哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1376595_comment'></div>既而巍巍峨峨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1376595_comment'></div>金辉铁牢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1376595_comment'></div>其东则翼以经藏焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1376595_comment'></div>其藏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1376595_comment'></div>外搆以扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1376595_comment'></div>八角两层。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1376595_comment'></div>刻栴檀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1376595_comment'></div>镂金铜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1376595_comment'></div>饰朱漆之炳焕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1376595_comment'></div>仍卫以华堂七间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1376595_comment'></div>名之转经焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1376595_comment'></div>致其沙门比邱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1376595_comment'></div>比比厥迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1376595_comment'></div>以为拜昌<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_178_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/178/Comments/0")'>趺读</span>丛谈聚听之凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1376595_comment'></div>日系乎月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1376595_comment'></div>月系乎时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1376595_comment'></div>轩轩阗阗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1376595_comment'></div>奚景福之不幽资乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1376595_comment'></div>又感应天王殿一间两厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1376595_comment'></div>其天王也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1376595_comment'></div>变毗沙之身于感通之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1376595_comment'></div>现神质为龟城之助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1376595_comment'></div>绦腰衣褐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1376595_comment'></div>屣足乘云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1376595_comment'></div>双吐目光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1376595_comment'></div>两飞霞彩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1376595_comment'></div>乃千百亿化身之一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1376595_comment'></div>为寿山草木之应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1376595_comment'></div>今塑于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1376595_comment'></div>厥感宁亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1376595_comment'></div>其西则翼之别殿曰塔殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1376595_comment'></div>其塔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1376595_comment'></div>我公萌誓愿之先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1376595_comment'></div>因心以制十有三层之妙形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1376595_comment'></div>匪伟而诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1376595_comment'></div>有为<span class='inlineComment2'>（去声）</span>殿斯奇而塔斯处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1376595_comment'></div>其北则报恩变相堂九间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1376595_comment'></div>洁琉璃之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1376595_comment'></div>等娑婆之世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1376595_comment'></div>七宝丛树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1376595_comment'></div>五色腾光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1376595_comment'></div>明明见阇提之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1376595_comment'></div>一一标如来之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1376595_comment'></div>又僧堂五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1376595_comment'></div>上五门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1376595_comment'></div>下之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1376595_comment'></div>与茶堂五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1376595_comment'></div>直联曲交。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1376595_comment'></div>冬温夏凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1376595_comment'></div>又华钟之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1376595_comment'></div>迥起青音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1376595_comment'></div>下折刀山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_217_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/217/Comments/0")'>长明灯</span>之台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1376595_comment'></div>圆笼孤光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1376595_comment'></div>杳辉漆壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1376595_comment'></div>其东南之臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1376595_comment'></div>复建地藏殿一间两厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1376595_comment'></div>功德堂五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1376595_comment'></div>僧堂五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1376595_comment'></div>张如别搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1376595_comment'></div>而制匪异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1376595_comment'></div>其殿也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1376595_comment'></div>坐以菩萨之丽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1376595_comment'></div>若欲飞动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1376595_comment'></div>其堂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1376595_comment'></div>骈错仪像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1376595_comment'></div>或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_231_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/231/Comments/0")'>金范</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1376595_comment'></div>或幅缋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1376595_comment'></div>千形百质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1376595_comment'></div>恐悉诸天之圣侣无间焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1376595_comment'></div>公厅四门一厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1376595_comment'></div>或备旌钺之觏止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1376595_comment'></div>我公或四季之旦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1376595_comment'></div>三旬之八。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1376595_comment'></div>聚僧设会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1376595_comment'></div>拜首追祝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1376595_comment'></div>勤勤恪恪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1376595_comment'></div>罔所不至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1376595_comment'></div>举闽之高卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1376595_comment'></div>举闽之少耋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1376595_comment'></div>攀之望之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1376595_comment'></div>无不动心涕臆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1376595_comment'></div>君子谓岂惟冥荐于先。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1376595_comment'></div>盖以孝教民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1376595_comment'></div>又库厨五间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1376595_comment'></div>浴室三间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1376595_comment'></div>接以井。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1376595_comment'></div>井重以楼焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1376595_comment'></div>环周辐辏之行廊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1376595_comment'></div>凡三十有三间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1376595_comment'></div>惣费财六万馀贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1376595_comment'></div>如山之謺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1376595_comment'></div>如洞之浚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1376595_comment'></div>巑巑隆隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1376595_comment'></div>丛为一宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1376595_comment'></div>其大也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1376595_comment'></div>琢文石以为轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1376595_comment'></div>雕修虹以为梁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1376595_comment'></div>其小也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1376595_comment'></div>取良木于灵山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1376595_comment'></div>筛嘉壤于飞尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1376595_comment'></div>虽掩映乎人间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1376595_comment'></div>实参差乎象外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1376595_comment'></div>其经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1376595_comment'></div>帙十卷于一函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1376595_comment'></div>凡五百四十有一函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1376595_comment'></div>惣五千四十有八卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1376595_comment'></div>皆极剡藤之精。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1376595_comment'></div>书工之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1376595_comment'></div>金轴锦带。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1376595_comment'></div>以为之饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1376595_comment'></div>天祐二年乙丑夏四月朔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1376595_comment'></div>我公宿诚于州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1376595_comment'></div>束烹于肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1376595_comment'></div>及胁降之辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1376595_comment'></div>大陈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_280_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/280/Comments/0")'>法会</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1376595_comment'></div>以藏其经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1376595_comment'></div>缁徒累千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1376595_comment'></div>士庶越万。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1376595_comment'></div>若缁若士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1376595_comment'></div>一而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1376595_comment'></div>正身<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_286_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/286/Comments/0")'>翔手</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1376595_comment'></div>右捧左授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1376595_comment'></div>自州之戺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1376595_comment'></div>起于我公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1376595_comment'></div>传至于藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1376595_comment'></div>观者如堵墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1376595_comment'></div>佛声入霄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1376595_comment'></div>幡花照乎全郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1376595_comment'></div>香烟连乎半空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_295_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/295/Comments/0")'>雪顶</span>之僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1376595_comment'></div>指西土之未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_297_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/297/Comments/0")'>骀背</span>之叟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1376595_comment'></div>庆东闽之天降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1376595_comment'></div>可谓之鸿因妙果者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1376595_comment'></div>始者我公之登坛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1376595_comment'></div>其一之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1376595_comment'></div>偃于戈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1376595_comment'></div>兴礼乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1376595_comment'></div>二之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1376595_comment'></div>陈耒耜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1376595_comment'></div>均<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_306_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/306/Comments/0")'>赋舆</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1376595_comment'></div>三之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1376595_comment'></div>謺贡输。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1376595_comment'></div>祇宠泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1376595_comment'></div>万乘臣其职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1376595_comment'></div>四邻视其睦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1376595_comment'></div>百姓天其政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1376595_comment'></div>故一川之镜如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1376595_comment'></div>灵台之月如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1376595_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_315_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/315/Comments/0")'>融融怡怡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1376595_comment'></div>愉愉熙熙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1376595_comment'></div>乃大读儒释之书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1376595_comment'></div>研古今之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1376595_comment'></div>常曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1376595_comment'></div>文武之与释氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1376595_comment'></div>盖同波而异流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1376595_comment'></div>若儒之五常仁义礼智信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1376595_comment'></div>仁者含宏也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1376595_comment'></div>比释之慈悲为之近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1376595_comment'></div>礼者谦让也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1376595_comment'></div>比释之恭敬为之近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1376595_comment'></div>智者通识也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1376595_comment'></div>比释之圣觉为之近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1376595_comment'></div>信者直诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1376595_comment'></div>比释之正直为之近。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1376595_comment'></div>而义者杀也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1376595_comment'></div>其为异诸武之七德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1376595_comment'></div>至如戢兵保大安民<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_333_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/333/Comments/0")'>和众</span>之类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1376595_comment'></div>亦犹川陆之徂秦适洛焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1376595_comment'></div>然则皆谓之烦恼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1376595_comment'></div>吾父国也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1376595_comment'></div>子民也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1376595_comment'></div>朝为社稷之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1376595_comment'></div>暮作稼穑之念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1376595_comment'></div>若俾求智慧火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1376595_comment'></div>乾烦恼海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1376595_comment'></div>则非吾之所能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1376595_comment'></div>若建金地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1376595_comment'></div>缮金文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1376595_comment'></div>陈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_345_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/345/Comments/0")'>法会</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1376595_comment'></div>一众僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1376595_comment'></div>冀乎不可思议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1376595_comment'></div>乃吾之所志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1376595_comment'></div>于是月陈三斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1376595_comment'></div>时或雪峰之僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1376595_comment'></div>围绕千徒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1376595_comment'></div>卧龙之僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1376595_comment'></div>围绕五百。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1376595_comment'></div>以至万钱之膳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1376595_comment'></div>或閒嘉蔬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1376595_comment'></div>五裤之歌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1376595_comment'></div>或参云梵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1376595_comment'></div>慈航驾岸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1376595_comment'></div>法雨垂空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1376595_comment'></div>必致菩萨化身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1376595_comment'></div>罗汉混俗以降也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1376595_comment'></div>时人谓灵山之会日俨矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1376595_comment'></div>又以府之寺至于清源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_363_1376595_comment'></div>或存或烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_364_1376595_comment'></div>或抽金积俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_365_1376595_comment'></div>增而新之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_366_1376595_comment'></div>而府之开元大中神光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_367_1376595_comment'></div>曩塔之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_368_1376595_comment'></div>与寺俱焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_369_1376595_comment'></div>新于大中神光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_370_1376595_comment'></div>乃规旧制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_371_1376595_comment'></div>而精㸌宏壮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_372_1376595_comment'></div>则迈前时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_373_1376595_comment'></div>开元则辅之经藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_374_1376595_comment'></div>加之转轮之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_375_1376595_comment'></div>尊大君也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_376_1376595_comment'></div>定光多宝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_377_1376595_comment'></div>报恩于劬劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_378_1376595_comment'></div>故以塼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_379_1376595_comment'></div>塼者专也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_380_1376595_comment'></div>谓山度之材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_381_1376595_comment'></div>有<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_382_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/382/Comments/0")'>蠹朽</span>之日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_382_1376595_comment'></div>火化之壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_383_1376595_comment'></div>无销铄之期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_384_1376595_comment'></div>其本乎土也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_385_1376595_comment'></div>资乎火也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_386_1376595_comment'></div>及投诸水火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_387_1376595_comment'></div>则不归乎土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_388_1376595_comment'></div>不坏于水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_389_1376595_comment'></div>历千秋而其质坚然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_390_1376595_comment'></div>乃以专至坚贞之诚寓于是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_391_1376595_comment'></div>则斯诚也如是得无感乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_392_1376595_comment'></div>则彼珠之为符验矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_393_1376595_comment'></div>且夫珠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_394_1376595_comment'></div>或颔乎龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_395_1376595_comment'></div>或衔乎蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_396_1376595_comment'></div>或胎乎蚌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_397_1376595_comment'></div>故水怀而川媚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_398_1376595_comment'></div>今兹珠也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_399_1376595_comment'></div>不自乎龙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_400_1376595_comment'></div>不自乎蛇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_401_1376595_comment'></div>不自乎蚌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_402_1376595_comment'></div>匪怀水而媚川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_403_1376595_comment'></div>而孕厚地之二十尺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_404_1376595_comment'></div>岂非斯之感欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_405_1376595_comment'></div>不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_406_1376595_comment'></div>则始从融结而孕之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_407_1376595_comment'></div>若以始从融结而孕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_408_1376595_comment'></div>则厥初已兆我唐之有我公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_409_1376595_comment'></div>厥初已兆我唐之有我公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_410_1376595_comment'></div>则我公之言乌石之有神光天王九仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_411_1376595_comment'></div>代虚其作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_412_1376595_comment'></div>地秘其期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_413_1376595_comment'></div>以待我信矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_414_1376595_comment'></div>塔之讫功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_415_1376595_comment'></div>顾小从事滔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_416_1376595_comment'></div>有礼官甲科之忝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_417_1376595_comment'></div>明主研许之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_418_1376595_comment'></div>庶哉于圣人立身扬名之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_419_1376595_comment'></div>命为之记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_420_1376595_comment'></div>用旌厥德于无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_421_1376595_comment'></div>滔不敢牢让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_422_1376595_comment'></div>作礼而推之言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_423_1376595_comment'></div>夫陶天地为后时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_424_1376595_comment'></div>销生死于无眹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_425_1376595_comment'></div>其道不可以真虚求声影赜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_426_1376595_comment'></div>应誓愿于有为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_427_1376595_comment'></div>现感通于至诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_428_1376595_comment'></div>其道乃可以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_429_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/429/Comments/0")'>精谛</span>至严敬致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_429_1376595_comment'></div>今我公以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_430_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/430/Comments/0")'>精谛</span>严敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_430_1376595_comment'></div>积功累德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_431_1376595_comment'></div>以溯流于世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_432_1376595_comment'></div>斯塔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_433_1376595_comment'></div>岳岳崇崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_434_1376595_comment'></div>兼乎仁孝之鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_435_1376595_comment'></div>偕天地日月江山之永。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_436_1376595_comment'></div>遂刻于贞石焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_437_1376595_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_438_1376595_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_439_1376595'>金圣人教德与功兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_439_1376595_comment'></div>鲁圣人教孝与忠兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_440_1376595_comment'></div>巍巍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_441_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/441/Comments/0")'>贤杰</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_441_1376595_comment'></div>二美钟兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_442_1376595_comment'></div>建兹宝塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_443_1376595_comment'></div>惟追崇兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_444_1376595_comment'></div>祝天沥恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_445_1376595_comment'></div>先延鸿兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_446_1376595_comment'></div>报劬荐祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_447_1376595_comment'></div>祈幽通兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_448_1376595_comment'></div>仙山之秀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_449_1376595_comment'></div>夷且隆兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_450_1376595_comment'></div>旷古为期。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_451_1376595_comment'></div>俟仁风兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_452_1376595_comment'></div>月圆珠现。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_453_1376595_comment'></div>契遭逢兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_454_1376595_comment'></div>融结之初。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_455_1376595_comment'></div>兆英雄兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_456_1376595_comment'></div>岂徒嶪嶪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_457_1376595_comment'></div>懿班工兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_458_1376595_comment'></div>火壤之贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_459_1376595_comment'></div>积磨砻兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_460_1376595_comment'></div>斧材之取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_461_1376595_comment'></div>厥匪同兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_462_1376595_comment'></div>七层八面。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_463_1376595_comment'></div>相玲珑兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_464_1376595_comment'></div>金铃宝铎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_465_1376595_comment'></div>交丁冬兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_466_1376595_comment'></div>影落澄清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_467_1376595_comment'></div>驯鱼龙兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_468_1376595_comment'></div>顶触圆碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_469_1376595_comment'></div>分鸿濛兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_470_1376595_comment'></div>缋仪范像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_471_1376595_comment'></div>謺其中兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_472_1376595_comment'></div>齐天极地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_473_1376595_comment'></div>为初终兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_474_1376595_comment'></div>金文<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_475_1376595", 1376595, "Clauses/475/Comments/0")'>贝字</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_475_1376595_comment'></div>搆重重兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_476_1376595_comment'></div>讲读千来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_477_1376595_comment'></div>罄西东兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_478_1376595_comment'></div>灵山盛会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_479_1376595_comment'></div>日雍雍兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_480_1376595_comment'></div>甘露法雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_481_1376595_comment'></div>常蒙茏兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_482_1376595_comment'></div>鸿名冥祉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_483_1376595_comment'></div>偕无穷兮。</div><div id='poem_sentence_484_1376595_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=906&endYear=906')">906年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=907&endYear=907')">907年1月</a>　王审知设二十万人无遮大会贺金铜佛像成，黄滔撰文记之。作品：《丈六金身碑》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376597' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376597' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376597?labeling=true' target='_blank'>丈六金身碑</a><span class='authorDate'>（907年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376597")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376597_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376597'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376597'>释氏之称释迦牟尼佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376597_comment'></div>千百亿化身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376597_comment'></div>而古今之世以诸佛菩萨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376597_comment'></div>其或铸成塑成刻成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376597_comment'></div>其或壁绘幅绘乎像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376597_comment'></div>不可胜纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376597_comment'></div>况多应现感通之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376597_comment'></div>自其非之乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376597_comment'></div>我公粤天祐三年丙寅秋七月乙丑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376597_comment'></div>铸金铜像一<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376597_comment'></div>丈有六尺之高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376597_comment'></div>后二十有三日丁亥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376597_comment'></div>继之铸菩萨二<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376597_comment'></div>丈有三尺高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376597_comment'></div>铜为内肌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376597_comment'></div>金为外肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376597_comment'></div>取法西天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376597_comment'></div>铸成东越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376597_comment'></div>巍巍落落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376597_comment'></div>毫光<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>法相</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376597_comment'></div>初我公登坛之三年己未秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376597_comment'></div>一夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376597_comment'></div>雨歇天清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376597_comment'></div>风微月明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376597_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>瑶兔</span>无烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376597_comment'></div>铜龙有声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376597_comment'></div>俄梦天之西际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376597_comment'></div>耀以照物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376597_comment'></div>䌽云罅裂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376597_comment'></div>大佛中座。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376597_comment'></div>岳岳以觏止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376597_comment'></div>熙熙而启言曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376597_comment'></div>断子一臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376597_comment'></div>卫之一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376597_comment'></div>既觉而思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376597_comment'></div>现乎形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376597_comment'></div>昭像也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376597_comment'></div>断一臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376597_comment'></div>誓诚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376597_comment'></div>卫一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376597_comment'></div>保众也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376597_comment'></div>始嘉其异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376597_comment'></div>姑默其事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376597_comment'></div>后创其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376597_comment'></div>乃命自<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>宾席</span>之逮将校。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376597_comment'></div>将校之逮步乘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376597_comment'></div>步乘之逮众庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376597_comment'></div>其有植信根之深者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376597_comment'></div>映惠烛之明者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376597_comment'></div>许一以金投吾俸中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376597_comment'></div>将椟于肆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376597_comment'></div>俟以铜易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376597_comment'></div>而后鸠工鸿炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376597_comment'></div>卜境择日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376597_comment'></div>铸斯佛于九仙山定光多宝塔之右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376597_comment'></div>古仙徐登上升之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376597_comment'></div>其日圆空镜然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376597_comment'></div>江山四爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376597_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_58_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/58/Comments/0")'>橐籥</span>之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376597_comment'></div>腾为烟云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376597_comment'></div>盘旋氤氲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376597_comment'></div>五色成文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376597_comment'></div>又有群鸟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376597_comment'></div>或若鸿鹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376597_comment'></div>或如莺鹊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376597_comment'></div>交翔而间鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376597_comment'></div>自寅而及午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376597_comment'></div>斯佛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376597_comment'></div>一泻而成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376597_comment'></div>翼日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376597_comment'></div>我公礼阅之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376597_comment'></div>乃与梦中一类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376597_comment'></div>其形仪长短大小无少差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376597_comment'></div>其一臂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376597_comment'></div>工以之别铸而会<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376597_comment'></div>我公神之而露其梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376597_comment'></div>于是迎入府之别亭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376597_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>磨莹</span>雕饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376597_comment'></div>克尽其妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376597_comment'></div>朝夕瞻拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376597_comment'></div>时不之怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376597_comment'></div>冬十有二月丙申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376597_comment'></div>会僧千千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376597_comment'></div>以幡以幢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376597_comment'></div>以钟以磬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376597_comment'></div>引归于开元寺寿山之塔院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376597_comment'></div>独殿以居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376597_comment'></div>翼二菩萨于左右。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376597_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_88_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/88/Comments/0")'>三十二相</span>足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376597_comment'></div>八十种好具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376597_comment'></div>螺累累以成髻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376597_comment'></div>珠隐隐以炫额。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376597_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>檀信</span>及门而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_92_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/92/Comments/1")'>膝地</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376597_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_93_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>童耋</span>遍城而掌胶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376597_comment'></div>夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376597_comment'></div>岂非千百亿化身之一乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376597_comment'></div>不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376597_comment'></div>焉得入乎梦而如乎神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376597_comment'></div>成乎形而如乎梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376597_comment'></div>梦不之告。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376597_comment'></div>工以之缺者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376597_comment'></div>其应现感通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376597_comment'></div>复为之殊矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376597_comment'></div>大矣哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376597_comment'></div>且先天地生之谓道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376597_comment'></div>后天地设之谓象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376597_comment'></div>道者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376597_comment'></div>以无为为志之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376597_comment'></div>授心印于虚空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376597_comment'></div>象者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376597_comment'></div>以有为为志之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376597_comment'></div>謺慧力于报应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376597_comment'></div>论者惑<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376597_comment'></div>以之为风马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376597_comment'></div>曾不谓象犹道之毂也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376597_comment'></div>无象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376597_comment'></div>道不行矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376597_comment'></div>始者摩腾竺法兰二梵僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376597_comment'></div>不慎其象东其道且西耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376597_comment'></div>惜乎不与三皇五帝同世而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376597_comment'></div>设与三皇五帝同世而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376597_comment'></div>必能从容朴素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376597_comment'></div>迟回仁义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376597_comment'></div>诈伪未之亟蠹也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376597_comment'></div>柰何天将后之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376597_comment'></div>岂徒然哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376597_comment'></div>岂不以仁义之生也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376597_comment'></div>曰尧与舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376597_comment'></div>仁义之亡也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376597_comment'></div>曰癸与受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376597_comment'></div>至于列国之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376597_comment'></div>强秦之立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376597_comment'></div>癸受之悖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376597_comment'></div>亹亹其躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376597_comment'></div>天谓仲尼祖述尧舜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376597_comment'></div>宪章文武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376597_comment'></div>终不能独制之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376597_comment'></div>故东释迦牟尼于中土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376597_comment'></div>大陈出生入死之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376597_comment'></div>天堂地法之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376597_comment'></div>以警戒之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376597_comment'></div>虽人世之风波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376597_comment'></div>万态逆翻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376597_comment'></div>而幽府之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_143_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/143/Comments/0")'>铁缧</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376597_comment'></div>一无苟免。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376597_comment'></div>上智闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376597_comment'></div>若镜之磨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376597_comment'></div>中智闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376597_comment'></div>若泉之澄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376597_comment'></div>下智闻之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376597_comment'></div>若火之烧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376597_comment'></div>谓之为有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376597_comment'></div>则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_152_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/152/Comments/0")'>河沙</span>芥子之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376597_comment'></div>虚诞难测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376597_comment'></div>谓之为无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1376597_comment'></div>则应现感通之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1376597_comment'></div>寻常立验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1376597_comment'></div>故能销嗜欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1376597_comment'></div>更祸福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1376597_comment'></div>一贵贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1376597_comment'></div>则为裨教化之一源。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1376597_comment'></div>湛然不动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1376597_comment'></div>感而遂通者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1376597_comment'></div>而以金厥地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1376597_comment'></div>莲厥宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1376597_comment'></div>张<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_165_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/165/Comments/0")'>法桥</span>以度人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1376597_comment'></div>无刑网以束俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1376597_comment'></div>世之敬之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1376597_comment'></div>怠之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1376597_comment'></div>黩之可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1376597_comment'></div>由是有以委之国君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1376597_comment'></div>委之大臣之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1376597_comment'></div>既而委之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1376597_comment'></div>则人非常人。<div id='poem_sentence_175_1376597_comment'></div>有神僧识。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1376597_comment'></div>仗钺之雄也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1376597_comment'></div>应江沙期。<div id='poem_sentence_180_1376597_comment'></div>契菩萨说<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1376597_comment'></div>夫通神为佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1376597_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_183_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/183/Comments/0")'>魂交</span>曰梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1376597_comment'></div>神非梦而罕通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1376597_comment'></div>梦非神而不感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1376597_comment'></div>我公之庆钟也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1376597_comment'></div>其如是矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1376597_comment'></div>其明年正月十有八日乙未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1376597_comment'></div>设二十万人斋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1376597_comment'></div>号<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_190_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/190/Comments/0")'>无遮</span>以落之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1376597_comment'></div>是日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1376597_comment'></div>䌽云缬天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1376597_comment'></div>甘露粒松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1376597_comment'></div>香花之气扑地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1376597_comment'></div>经梵之声入空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1376597_comment'></div>座客有右省常侍陇西李公洵翰林承旨制诰兵部侍郎昌黎韩公偓中书舍人琅琊王公涤右补阙博陵崔徵君道融大司农琅琊王公标吏部郎中谯国夏侯公淑司勋员外郎王公拯刑部员外郎宏农杨公承休宏文馆直学士宏农杨公赞图宏文馆直学士琅琊王公倜集贤殿校理吴郡归公传懿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1376597_comment'></div>皆以文学之奥比<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_197_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/197/Comments/0")'>偃商</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1376597_comment'></div>侍从之声齐褒向。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1376597_comment'></div>甲乙升第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1376597_comment'></div>岩廊<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_200_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/200/Comments/0")'>韫望</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1376597_comment'></div>东浮荆襄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1376597_comment'></div>南游吴楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1376597_comment'></div>谓安莫安于闽越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1376597_comment'></div>诚莫诚于我公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1376597_comment'></div>依刘表。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1376597_comment'></div>起襄汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1376597_comment'></div>其地也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1376597_comment'></div>交辙及馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1376597_comment'></div>值斯佛之成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1376597_comment'></div>斯会之设。<div class='inline' 1376597, "Clauses/212/Comments/0")'>意马</span>于清凉山中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1376597_comment'></div>我公乃顾幕下者滔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1376597_comment'></div>俾刻贞石以碑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1376597_comment'></div>滔以甲科忝第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1376597_comment'></div>盛府蒙招。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1376597_comment'></div>刊勒之职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1376597_comment'></div>不敢牢让。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1376597_comment'></div>谨推于厥旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1376597_comment'></div>经云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1376597_comment'></div>作佛像之功德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1376597_comment'></div>斗量海以有尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1376597_comment'></div>尘碎劫以无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1376597_comment'></div>戏为之而以草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1376597_comment'></div>思见之而刻旃檀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1376597_comment'></div>其犹蜕现其生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1376597_comment'></div>羽金其报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1376597_comment'></div>而况今乃俨至诚。<div id='poem_sentence_232_1376597_comment'></div>金乎千千。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1376597_comment'></div>虔鼓铸于神仙之山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1376597_comment'></div>卜贞吉于火土之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1376597_comment'></div>其积功累德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1376597_comment'></div>岂可以边以涯而言之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1376597_comment'></div>或曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1376597_comment'></div>梁武帝之隆释氏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1376597_comment'></div>今古靡伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1376597_comment'></div>奚报应之昧乎。<div id='poem_sentence_243_1376597_comment'></div>不隆释氏之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1376597_comment'></div>所以然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1376597_comment'></div>夫帝王之道<span id='poem_sentence_250_1376597_comment'></div>故一夫不获。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1376597_comment'></div>若已陨诸隍中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1376597_comment'></div>此济度于触类。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1376597_comment'></div>故欲凡一有情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1376597_comment'></div>悉皆成佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1376597_comment'></div>梁武帝则不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1376597_comment'></div>以民之财之力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1376597_comment'></div>刹将三百。<div id='poem_sentence_260_1376597_comment'></div>削顶颔以言觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1376597_comment'></div>所以私所以然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1376597_comment'></div>今我公为邦则忠孝于君亲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1376597_comment'></div>牧人则父母于生民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1376597_comment'></div>造塔四。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1376597_comment'></div>其一曰寿山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1376597_comment'></div>以昭皇帝辛酉岁西巡。<div id='poem_sentence_271_1376597_comment'></div>其三其四大中神光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1376597_comment'></div>为军旅也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1376597_comment'></div>为人民也。<div id='poem_sentence_276_1376597_comment'></div>其三附于寿山定光大王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1376597_comment'></div>意同乎塔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1376597_comment'></div>月三其斋。<div id='poem_sentence_281_1376597_comment'></div>疏乎诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1376597_comment'></div>首则君亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1376597_comment'></div>次则军旅人民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1376597_comment'></div>而已后焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1376597_comment'></div>况斯佛已之而不已。<div class='inline'
