id='poem_sentence_287_1376597_comment'></div>故其地出明珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1376597_comment'></div>海出珊瑚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1376597_comment'></div>几于莲花妙品之繁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1376597_comment'></div>车渠玛瑙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1376597_comment'></div>幡幢璎珞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1376597_comment'></div>周乎多宝之涌也<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑷</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1376597_comment'></div>夫其元贶之如彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1376597_comment'></div>灵感之若此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1376597_comment'></div>则断一臂卫一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1376597_comment'></div>斯昭昭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1376597_comment'></div>岂与彼而论哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1376597_comment'></div>某是辄奋笔而无愧为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1376597_comment'></div>其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1376597_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_301_1376597'>托人佳梦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1376597_comment'></div>铸成鸿炉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1376597_comment'></div>毫光<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_303_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/303/Comments/0")'>法相</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1376597_comment'></div>铜肌金肤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1376597_comment'></div>恍惚现形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1376597_comment'></div>昭彰合符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1376597_comment'></div>不有为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1376597_comment'></div>其如是乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1376597_comment'></div>唐一其宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1376597_comment'></div>越百其区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1376597_comment'></div>伊闽之设。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1376597_comment'></div>于地之殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1376597_comment'></div>西城瓯仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1376597_comment'></div>东堑鳌隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1376597_comment'></div>匪德莫处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1376597_comment'></div>惟仁靡逾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1376597_comment'></div>懿其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_317_1376597", 1376597, "Clauses/317/Comments/0")'>橐籥</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1376597_comment'></div>飞作醍醐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1376597_comment'></div>焦山草木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1376597_comment'></div>不得不苏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1376597_comment'></div>苦海波澜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1376597_comment'></div>不得不枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1376597_comment'></div>仙花罔谢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1376597_comment'></div>慧日宁徂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1376597_comment'></div>永兹一方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1376597_comment'></div>盘石其都。</div><div id='poem_sentence_326_1376597_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1376597'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_74_1376597_0'>⑴ 其像大工虑其不就计以一臂别铸而会之乃暗符梦中</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_181_1376597_0'>⑵ 初丙午岁我公至清源未在时有僧号涅槃于众中骇而指之曰金轮王之第三子降人间幸勉之专生杀柄又闽之侯未尝至宰辅晋时郭璞记曰南台江沙合即有宰辅相我公之登台席也江沙契焉又梁时王霸怡山上升山在府城之西五里光启丁未岁衢之烂柯山道士徐景立因于其仙坛东北隅取土掘得瓷瓶七口各可容一升水其中悉有炭上总盖一青砖刻文字云树枯不用伐坛坏不须结未满一千岁自有系孙列后来是三皇潮水荡祸殃岩逢一乍开未免有销亡子孙依吾道代代封闽疆其坛东南有皂荚树古云真君于此树上上升其后枯矣至咸通庚寅岁复荣茂也又妫山僧号大安顷坐西禅者乾符中曰府城之到九仙三桥其中乃菩萨行化今之新城及焉</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_263_1376597_0'>⑶ 自兴兵以来天下以三司之泉皆名直进独我公以俸钱为直进三司之运悉如旧焉阙廷大称其美</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_293_1376597_0'>⑷ 开元定塔基掘地丈有五尺之深得宝珠上以金钱又于海中得珊瑚树凡二百馀株矣</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1376597_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=907&endYear=907')">907年3月</a>　崔道融卒，灵柩北返，黄滔撰文祭之。作品：《祭崔补阙道融》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=907&endYear=907')">907年</a>　朱温征罗隐为右谏议大夫，隐不至，终授给事中。黄滔写诗赞之。作品：《寄罗郎中隐》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_47455' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47455' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47455?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄罗郎中隐</a><span class='authorDate'>（907年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47455")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47455_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_47455'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5112, "poem_allusion_47455")'>九转</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_47455_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47455'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47455'>休向中兴雪至冤，钱塘江上看涛翻。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47455'>三徵不起时贤议，<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(5112, "poem_sentence_1_47455")'>九转</span>终成道者言。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47455'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_47455", 47455, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>绿酒</span>千杯肠已烂，新诗数首骨犹存。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47455'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_47455", 47455, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>瑶蟾</span>若使知人事，仙桂应遭蠹却根。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47455_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47455'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47455_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=908&endYear=908')">908年</a>　居王审知幕，为福州雪峰山故真觉大师撰碑铭。作品：《福州雪峰山故真觉大师碑铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376601' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376601' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376601?labeling=true' target='_blank'>福州雪峰山故真觉大师碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（908年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376601")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376601_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376601'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376601'>大师法号义存。长庆二年壬寅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376601_comment'></div>生于泉州南安县曾氏。自王父而下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376601_comment'></div>皆友僧亲佛。清净<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>谨志</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376601_comment'></div>大师生而鼻逆薰血。乳抱中或闻钟磬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376601_comment'></div>或见僧佛。其容必动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376601_comment'></div>以是别钟爱于膝下。九岁请出家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376601_comment'></div>叶而未即。十二从家君游莆田玉涧寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376601_comment'></div>寺有律僧庆元。持行高洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376601_comment'></div>遽拜之曰。我师也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376601_comment'></div>遂留为童子焉。十七落发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376601_comment'></div>淳朴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>贞古</span>。了与流辈异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376601_comment'></div>暨武宗皇帝乙丑之否。乃束发于儒冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376601_comment'></div>莱中而蓬迹。来府之芙蓉山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376601_comment'></div>宏照大师见奇之。故止其所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376601_comment'></div>至宣宗皇帝之复其道也。涅而不缁其身也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376601_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>褎然</span>而出。北游吴楚梁宋燕秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376601_comment'></div>受具足戒于幽州宝刹寺讫。巡名山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376601_comment'></div>扣诸禅宗。突兀飘飖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376601_comment'></div>云翔鸟游。爰及武陵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376601_comment'></div>一面德山。止于珍重而出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376601_comment'></div>其徒数百。咸莫之测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376601_comment'></div>德山曰。斯无偕也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376601_comment'></div>吾得之矣。咸通六年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376601_comment'></div>师归于芙蓉之故山。其年圆寂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376601_comment'></div>大师亦自沩山拥徒至。坐于怡山王真君上升之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376601_comment'></div>其徒熟<span class='inlineComment2'>（熟师已嗣德山）</span>累累而关。师拒而久之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376601_comment'></div>则有行实者。始以师同而议曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376601_comment'></div>师之近巍巍乎。法门围绕之所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376601_comment'></div>不可造次。其地宜若鹫岭猴江之为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376601_comment'></div>卜府之西二百里有山焉。环控四邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376601_comment'></div>峭拔万仞。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>崷崒</span>以支圆碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376601_comment'></div>培塿以覛群青。怪石古松。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376601_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>栖蛰</span>龟鹤。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/65/Comments/0")'>灵湫</span>邃壑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376601_comment'></div>隐见<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/66/Comments/0")'>龙雷</span>山之半。顶之上则先冬而雪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376601_comment'></div>盛夏而寒。其树皆别垂藤萝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376601_comment'></div>䒠茸而以为之衣。交错而不呈其形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376601_comment'></div>奇姿异景。不可殚状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376601_comment'></div>虽霍童武夷。无以加之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376601_comment'></div>实闽越之神秀。而古仙之未攸居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376601_comment'></div>诚有待于我师也。祈以偕行<span class='inlineComment2'>（去声）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376601_comment'></div>秋七月。穿云蹑藓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376601_comment'></div>陟险升幽。将及之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376601_comment'></div>师曰。真吾居也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376601_comment'></div>其夕。山之神果效灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376601_comment'></div>翼日。岩谷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_44_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/89/Comments/0")'>爽朗</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376601_comment'></div>烟霞飞动。云庵既立。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376601_comment'></div>月构旋隆。繇是柅法轮于无为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376601_comment'></div>树空门于有地。行实乃请名其山曰雪峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376601_comment'></div>以其冬雪夏寒。取鹫岭猴江之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376601_comment'></div>斯则庚寅。逮于乙未。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376601_comment'></div>师以山而道侔。山以师而名出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376601_comment'></div>天下之释子。不计华夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376601_comment'></div>趋之如赴召。乾符中观察使京兆韦公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376601_comment'></div>中和中司空颍川陈公。每渴醍醐而不克就饮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376601_comment'></div>交使<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>驰恳</span>。师为之入府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376601_comment'></div>从人愿也。其时内官有复命于京。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376601_comment'></div>语其道。其侪之拔俗悟空者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376601_comment'></div>请蜕浮华而来薙。僖宗皇帝闻之翰林学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376601_comment'></div>访于闽人陈延郊。得其实奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376601_comment'></div>于是圣锡真觉大师之号。仍以紫袈裟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376601_comment'></div>俾延郊授焉。大师授之如不授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376601_comment'></div>衣之如不衣。居累夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376601_comment'></div>辛亥岁朔。遽然杖履。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376601_comment'></div>其徒启而不答。云以随之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376601_comment'></div>东浮于丹邱四明。明年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376601_comment'></div>故府侍中之有无诸□尅<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>洗兵于法雨。致敬于禅林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376601_comment'></div>馥师之道。常东望顶手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376601_comment'></div>后二年。自吴还闽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376601_comment'></div>大加礼异。今闽王誓众养民之外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376601_comment'></div>雅隆其道。凡斋僧构刹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376601_comment'></div>以之龟焉。为之增宇设像。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376601_comment'></div>铸钟以严其山。优施以充其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376601_comment'></div>时则迎而馆之于府之东西甲第。每将俨油幢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376601_comment'></div>聆法轮。未尝不移时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376601_comment'></div>馀乎一纪。勤勤恳恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376601_comment'></div>熊罴之士。因之投迹檀𨚗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376601_comment'></div>渔猎之逸。其或弭心鳞羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376601_comment'></div>戊辰年春三月示疾。吾王走医。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376601_comment'></div>医至。粒药以授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376601_comment'></div>师曰。吾非疾也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376601_comment'></div>不可罔子之工。卒不之饵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376601_comment'></div>其后札偈以遗法子。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/163/Comments/0")'>函翰</span>以别王庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376601_comment'></div>夏五月二日。鸟兽悲鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376601_comment'></div>云水<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_83_1376601", 1376601, "Clauses/166/Comments/0")'>惨悴</span>。其夜十有八刻时灭度。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376601_comment'></div>俗八十有七。僧腊五十有九。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376601_comment'></div>以其月十五日塔其藏焉。其塔也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376601_comment'></div>其徒佥云。以山之奇堂之峻<span class='inlineComment2'>（法堂也）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376601_comment'></div>大师之生也<span class='inlineComment2'>（去声）</span>。是其殁也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376601_comment'></div>不宜舍诸。故坎其中焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376601_comment'></div>若干尺之高。若干尺之周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376601_comment'></div>皆雕珉石。错火壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376601_comment'></div>磷磷焉。嶪嶪焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376601_comment'></div>四隅则环宇以庥。玲珑䆗窱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376601_comment'></div>云霞时入。风雨罔侵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376601_comment'></div>其日奔闽之僧尼士庶。仅五千人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376601_comment'></div>闽王娣之子降左金吾卫将军检校刑部尚书延禀。始陈祭是设斋焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376601_comment'></div>大矣哉。大师之见世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376601_comment'></div>于是罔量其僧耶。自始及兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376601_comment'></div>凡四十年。东西南北之夏往秋适者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376601_comment'></div>不可胜纪。而常不减一千五百徒之环足其趋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376601_comment'></div>驰而愈离。辩而愈惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376601_comment'></div>常曰。三世诸佛十二分教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376601_comment'></div>到此乃徒劳耳。其庶几者若干人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376601_comment'></div>其一号师备。拥徒于元沙<span class='inlineComment2'>（今安国也）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376601_comment'></div>其二号可休。拥徒于越州洞岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376601_comment'></div>其三号智孚。拥徒于信州鹅湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376601_comment'></div>其四号慧棱。拥徒于泉州招庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376601_comment'></div>其五号神晏。今府之鼓山也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376601_comment'></div>分灯之道。皆膺圣奖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376601_comment'></div>锡紫袈裟。而元沙级宗一大师招庆元晤大师鼓山定慧大师之命焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376601_comment'></div>其曹早曰。法虽无说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376601_comment'></div>名以文垂。自少林之建曹溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376601_comment'></div>无不刻碑而纪颂。我师其默乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376601_comment'></div>一旦惣其曹<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>。首曰从智如堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376601_comment'></div>而扣愚求文。滔老且病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376601_comment'></div>刊勒之加。多已辞避。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376601_comment'></div>钦师之道。不觉耸然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376601_comment'></div>伟夫。恭闻释波之东注也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376601_comment'></div>流其象则不流其旨。流其旨则不象其形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376601_comment'></div>厥初大迦叶之垂二十八叶。至于达摩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376601_comment'></div>达摩六叶。止于曹溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376601_comment'></div>分宗南北。德山则南宗五叶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376601_comment'></div>大师嗣<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>。其今六叶焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376601_comment'></div>雪峰之分元沙洞岩鹅湖招庆鼓山。其道皆离贝叶以祗其七。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376601_comment'></div>非滔之能言也。但美数公葳蕤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376601_comment'></div>其叶众多。殷勤之请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376601_comment'></div>遂为之铭而应其求。其词曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376601_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_127_1376601'>曹溪分派。谁继南宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376601_comment'></div>一言冠绝。六叶推雄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376601_comment'></div>无物之物。非空之空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376601_comment'></div>不莹而明。不增而隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376601_comment'></div>缩靡秋毫。舒靡鸿濛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376601_comment'></div>不有灵镜。曷扬真风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376601_comment'></div>懿彼闽越。巍乎一峰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376601_comment'></div>洞壑斯异。雪霜罕同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376601_comment'></div>天之有待。师也云钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376601_comment'></div>名将道协。迹与仙崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376601_comment'></div>奔走厥徒。百千其丛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376601_comment'></div>庶几几人。莫不元通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376601_comment'></div>分灯照耀。树本玲珑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376601_comment'></div>圣君宠謺。贤王敬重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376601_comment'></div>不生不灭。曷始曷终。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376601_comment'></div>刻贞石于斯文。旌厥德于梵宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376601_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_143_1376601_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
莆田

id='poem_sentence_1_47440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47440'>新诗说人尽，旧宅落花频。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47440_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=897&endYear=897')">897年</a>　居家。作品：《送外甥翁袭明赴举序》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376581' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376581' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376581?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送外甥翁袭明赴举序</a><span class='authorDate'>（897年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376581")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376581_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376581'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376581'>诗言简。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376581_comment'></div>赋词饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376581_comment'></div>不可以叙事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376581_comment'></div>故若之行也送以序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376581_comment'></div>袭明早举童子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376581_comment'></div>旧儒因以小松为之目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376581_comment'></div>袭明默而思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376581_comment'></div>松之小者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376581_comment'></div>干霄之势则尔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376581_comment'></div>搆厦之用则否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376581_comment'></div>推是言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376581_comment'></div>龆而一飞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376581_comment'></div>不若冠而十上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376581_comment'></div>乃退硕乎业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376581_comment'></div>果以词学擅州里誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376581_comment'></div>洎中兴之十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376581_comment'></div>寒进亹亹于科第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376581_comment'></div>袭明业东而迹不西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376581_comment'></div>惜违亲也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376581_comment'></div>近吾姊以他人之继翔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376581_comment'></div>念袭明之久蟠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376581_comment'></div>悄焉如疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376581_comment'></div>吾得以与内外之亲辈流之善者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376581_comment'></div>日激其行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376581_comment'></div>旋振于府帅州牧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376581_comment'></div>遂不得留于膝下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376581_comment'></div>大哉吾唐之设科第也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376581_comment'></div>实本于乡举里选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376581_comment'></div>乡举里选。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376581_comment'></div>莫不以忠孝先之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376581_comment'></div>繇是诸侯之岁贡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376581_comment'></div>其觯云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376581_comment'></div>忠于国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376581_comment'></div>孝于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376581_comment'></div>内则闺门和。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376581_comment'></div>外则乡党附。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376581_comment'></div>今袭明孝于家也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376581_comment'></div>闺门和也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376581_comment'></div>乡党附也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376581_comment'></div>而移孝于忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376581_comment'></div>中兴之第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376581_comment'></div>吾庆有司之得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376581_comment'></div>非庆袭明得也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376581_comment'></div>矧词学擅誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376581_comment'></div>前辈梗于公道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376581_comment'></div>或一倍两倍孙宏之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376581_comment'></div>今辈利于公道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376581_comment'></div>无再献三献卞和之泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376581_comment'></div>若其勉诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376581_comment'></div>高堂之违。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376581_comment'></div>吾知不及荐闰。</div><div id='poem_sentence_50_1376581_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='ae6b4df1d5644f3f9642993094454be5_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ae6b4df1d5644f3f9642993094454be5");'><span id='ae6b4df1d5644f3f9642993094454be5_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=909&endYear=911')">909-911年</a>，70-72岁</div><div id='ae6b4df1d5644f3f9642993094454be5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=909&endYear=909')">909年4月</a>　辞官居家。翁文尧以户部员外郎充闽王册礼副使使闽，王审知赐金紫，改乡里名号。滔为诗荣之。作品：《奉和翁文尧十九员外中谢日蒙恩赐金紫之什》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《翁文尧员外捧金紫还乡之命雅发篇章将原交情远为嘉贶洎燕鸿陆犬楚水荆山又吐琼瑶逮之幽鄙涌泉思触逸兴皆虚而强韵押难非才颇愧辄兹酬和以质奖私》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《奉和翁文尧员外经过七林书堂见寄之什》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《奉酬翁文尧员外驻南台见寄之什》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《翁文尧员外拥册礼之归一路有诗名昼锦集先将寄示因书五十六字》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《奉和翁文尧员外文秀光贤昼锦之什》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《奉酬翁文尧员外神泉之游见寄嘉什》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《送翁员外承赞》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_47391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉和翁文尧十九员外中谢日蒙恩赐金紫之什</a><span class='authorDate'>（909年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47391")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47391_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_47391'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9596, "poem_allusion_47391")'>严助</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_47391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47391'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47391'>面蒙君赐自龙墀，谁是还乡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_47391", 47391, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>一袭</span>衣。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47391'>三品易悬鳞鬣赫，八丝展起䌽章飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47391'>夐为胜事垂千古，题作新诗启七微。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47391'><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(9596, "poem_sentence_3_47391")'>严助</span>买臣精魄在，定应羞著<span class='inlineComment2'>（廷略反）</span>昔年归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47391'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47391_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_47436' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47436' class='poemTitle id='poem_sentence_4_47424'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47424_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=910&endYear=910')">910年</a>　辞官居家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=911&endYear=911')">911年3月</a>　辞官居家，为王审知撰文祭南平王刘隐。约本年卒。作品：《祭南海南平王》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376612' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376612' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376612?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭南海南平王<span class='inlineComment2'>（代闽王）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（911年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376612")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376612_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376612'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376612'>故南平王之灵。惟灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376612_comment'></div>五羊奥区。番禺巨壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376612_comment'></div>汉为列郡。唐作雄藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376612_comment'></div>总百蛮五岭之殷。有出将入相之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376612_comment'></div>是故地启嘉数。天生大贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376612_comment'></div>浚六韬三略之才谋。韫五裤二天之政术。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376612_comment'></div>俾其于家受诏。衣锦𧜗牙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376612_comment'></div>控二十四州之繁难。当二十八齿之美茂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376612_comment'></div>光扬千古。冠绝一时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376612_comment'></div>钟其明灵。其昭昭矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376612_comment'></div>至若恢张霸业。扬清波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376612_comment'></div>台陟九层。靡惭郭隗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376612_comment'></div>剑提三尺。授自吕虔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376612_comment'></div>爰持<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/26/Comments/0")'>副贰</span>之雄姿。遂领节旄之重寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376612_comment'></div>由是泽施甘露。令肃秋霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376612_comment'></div>掀文房武库以连云。腾逸气英风而偃草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376612_comment'></div>上榻则阮瑀。下贤则左车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376612_comment'></div>从善则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_17_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/34/Comments/0")'>轼闾</span>。宣威则断案。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376612_comment'></div>故得越伏波之铜柱。献而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376612_comment'></div>感鄂公之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>铁鞭</span>。呈祥以见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376612_comment'></div>火山改色。珠浦生光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376612_comment'></div>无烦处默之酌泉。大鄙赵陀之累土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376612_comment'></div>然后鸣钟出入。调鼎升闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376612_comment'></div>致交趾之封疆。归石门之教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376612_comment'></div>九迁渥泽。克居浴凤之池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376612_comment'></div>双立节旄。远过<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_25_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/51/Comments/0")'>跕鸢</span>之水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376612_comment'></div>虽士鲔列弟兄三地。山简兼荆湘四州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376612_comment'></div>语未同年。事推旷世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376612_comment'></div>呜呼。是何才德之若彼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376612_comment'></div>功业之如此。而彼穹者天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376612_comment'></div>不寿其齿。毕云龙之契会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376612_comment'></div>与龟鹤而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>等伦</span>。矧天子方欲使降皇华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376612_comment'></div>恩宣金册。表里东周之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376612_comment'></div>旌崇南越之隆。胡二竖之亟攻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376612_comment'></div>竟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_34_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/68/Comments/0")'>三医</span>之莫救。泰山颓坏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376612_comment'></div>俄兴孔氏之歌。汉水凄凉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376612_comment'></div>遽罢羊公之市。实国家之不幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376612_comment'></div>实藩镇之不幸。某早尘兴国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376612_comment'></div>旋忝睦邻。虽琼树之未亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376612_comment'></div>若铜盘之已接。方定金兰之至分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376612_comment'></div>岂期幽显之骤殊。况以幸结良姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376612_comment'></div>累交专介。幕下崔员外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376612_comment'></div>昨驰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/84/Comments/0")'>礼币</span>。尝诣门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376612_comment'></div>爰蒙执手之欢。宏叙亲仁之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376612_comment'></div>今则遽悲存殁。益叹彭殇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376612_comment'></div>故将荐举征尘。躬申薄奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376612_comment'></div>九泉<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/92/Comments/0")'>注望</span>。于叹逝以难胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376612_comment'></div>五月指期。表同盟之必至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376612_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。曩驰羔雁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376612_comment'></div>今遣蘋蘩。伊人事之有兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376612_comment'></div>顾痛伤而何极。然则荀龙贾虎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376612_comment'></div>大冯小冯。虽嗟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_51_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/103/Comments/0")'>松垄</span>之长归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376612_comment'></div>终庆荆枝而继茂。永言欢好。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376612_comment'></div>宁怠初终。幸明灵之一临。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376612_comment'></div>鉴此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_54_1376612", 1376612, "Clauses/108/Comments/0")'>丹赤</span>。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376612_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1376612_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
西安

id='poem_title_47367_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47367'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47367'>昨夜孤灯下，阑干泣数行。<div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=872&endYear=872')">872年</a>　约本年在京首应进士第，下第，有文谒侯圭。作品：《侯博士圭启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376555' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376555_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376555'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376555'>滔口讽雄词。心祈藻鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376555_comment'></div>在他处则早逾一纪。来上国则己逮二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376555_comment'></div>常<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376555", 1376555, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>测管</span>以推诚。每<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376555", 1376555, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>持蠡</span>而注念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376555_comment'></div>岂期御李。非敢希颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376555_comment'></div>所以窃贽荒芜。荐尘墙仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376555_comment'></div>耸蚁封于邱岳。疏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1376555", 1376555, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>蛙渚</span>于陂湖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376555_comment'></div>敢望吹嘘。伫聆诮责。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376555_comment'></div>昨日进士林郁。忽传尊旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376555_comment'></div>遽话殊私。伏惟博士曲降恩知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376555_comment'></div>俯回奖录。不置盖瓯之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376555_comment'></div>爰兴<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_1376555", 1376555, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>读蜺</span>之言。事迈常伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376555_comment'></div>荣过始望。倾身拜命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376555_comment'></div>跼影瞻风。若听咸韶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376555_comment'></div>如吞甘醴。敢便认为知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376555_comment'></div>盖将决定胸襟。实以当今文教风行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376555_comment'></div>词人辐辏。莫不俱陈素业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376555_comment'></div>各务所归。而博士负掷地鸿名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376555_comment'></div>标掞天逸势。吐扬雄之五藏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376555_comment'></div>陋班固之两京。故其接踵望尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376555_comment'></div>骈肩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376555", 1376555, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>执刺</span>。争为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376555", 1376555, "Clauses/39/Comments/0")'>秤挂</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376555_comment'></div>互作镜窥。或闻由也升堂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376555_comment'></div>赐之入室。是则千门改观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376555_comment'></div>万户飞声。若瑶璧之饰来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376555_comment'></div>类金丝而振作。所谓功侔造化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376555_comment'></div>言系惨舒。作词林培植之家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376555_comment'></div>为陆海梯航之主。必当不私其一顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376555_comment'></div>误彼众闻。以滔数载辛勤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376555_comment'></div>一生疑惑。唯倾丹恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376555_comment'></div>翘瞩重言。冀将卜以妍媸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376555_comment'></div>断其可否。今则出于门馆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376555_comment'></div>发自齿牙。事既殊常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376555_comment'></div>道方自信。㭊<span class='inlineComment2'>（音倏）</span>同寐觉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376555_comment'></div>夐若神通。呈材之获般窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376555_comment'></div>鬻马之蒙乐顾。已逢哲匠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376555_comment'></div>肯愧他人。蜀壁端居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376555_comment'></div>管床兀坐。既佩兹<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1376555", 1376555, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>謦欬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376555_comment'></div>益励彼颛愚。苟无疑于镂冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376555_comment'></div>则求工于刻楮。忭跃兢悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376555_comment'></div>罔知所裁。下情无任感恩激切之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376555_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1376555_comment'></div></div></div><br ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=875&endYear=875')">875年1月</a>　应试。作品：《省试一一吹竽》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《省试王者之道如龙首赋》<span onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_47513", 47513, "Clauses/0/Comments/1")'>齐竽</span></span>今历试，真伪不难知。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47513'>欲使声声别，须令<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_47513", 47513, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>个个</span>吹。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47513'>后先无错杂，能否立参差。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47513'>次第教单进，宫商乃异宜。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47513'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_47513", 47513, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>凡音</span>皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_47513", 47513, "Clauses/8/Comments/1")'>窜迹</span>，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_47513", 47513, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>至艺</span>始<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_47513", 47513, "Clauses/9/Comments/1")'>呈奇</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_47513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_47513'>以此论文学，终凭一一窥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_47513_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_47513'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_47513_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376541' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376541' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376541?labeling=true' target='_blank'>省试王者之道如龙首赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以龙之视听有符君德为韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（875年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376541")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376541_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376541'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376541'>王者以御彼万国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376541_comment'></div>居于九重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376541_comment'></div>既<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376541", 1376541, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>体天</span>而立制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376541_comment'></div>遂如首以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1376541", 1376541, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>犹龙</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376541_comment'></div>视听无偏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376541_comment'></div>四海自看其波凑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376541_comment'></div>聪明罔失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376541_comment'></div>兆民咸睹其云从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376541_comment'></div>岂非<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376541", 1376541, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>祖述</span>圣明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376541_comment'></div>披陈道德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376541_comment'></div>以王者为天下之大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376541_comment'></div>域中之式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376541_comment'></div>非澄耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376541_comment'></div>不可以烛暗通幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376541_comment'></div>非审细微。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376541_comment'></div>不可以开基建极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376541_comment'></div>于是设喻斯异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376541_comment'></div>微文特殊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376541_comment'></div>以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1376541", 1376541, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>端拱</span>之尊比义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376541_comment'></div>取产泽之灵合符。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376541_comment'></div>则而象之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376541_comment'></div>既不雷同于形质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376541_comment'></div>区以别矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376541_comment'></div>爰将首冠于寰区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376541_comment'></div>然后岳岳高居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376541_comment'></div>禺禺克定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376541_comment'></div>翼左右而何惭角耸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376541_comment'></div>镜远近而宛同神莹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376541_comment'></div>虽云黈纩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376541_comment'></div>洪纤之状咸观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376541_comment'></div>纵使垂旒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376541_comment'></div>巨细之音毕听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376541_comment'></div>则知播雍熙之化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376541_comment'></div>为昭圣之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376541_comment'></div>遽配腾骧于水物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376541_comment'></div>益彰超迈于人群。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376541_comment'></div>浚恩波而固类兴雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376541_comment'></div>呈瑞气而非同召云。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376541_comment'></div>侔其矫举之形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376541_comment'></div>无幽不鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376541_comment'></div>媲彼孤标之貌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376541_comment'></div>有象皆分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376541_comment'></div>故得迥拔可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376541_comment'></div>感通自有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376541_comment'></div>散皇明而珠耀于颔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376541_comment'></div>扬德泽而浪生于口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376541_comment'></div>宁同荀爽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376541_comment'></div>只擅美于弟兄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376541_comment'></div>更异华歆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376541_comment'></div>但垂名于朋友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376541_comment'></div>所谓表有截。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376541_comment'></div>播无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376541_comment'></div>乃蔼然而同德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376541_comment'></div>非蠢尔以呈姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376541_comment'></div>言乎汉祖之颜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376541_comment'></div>方能比也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376541_comment'></div>念彼伯阳之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376541_comment'></div>未可方之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376541_comment'></div>今我后变见乘时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376541_comment'></div>飞翔叶理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376541_comment'></div>四方尽入于倾听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376541_comment'></div>陆海无遗于俯视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376541_comment'></div>夫如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376541_comment'></div>则龙之首兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376541_comment'></div>未可论功而较美。</div><div id='poem_sentence_64_1376541_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=875&endYear=875')">875年</a>　干谒郑諴，约代郑諴上书卢携。作品：《代郑郎中上静恭卢相启？》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376560' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376560' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376560?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑郎中上静恭卢相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（875年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376560")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376560_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376560'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376560'>伏以天覆地载。纵鬼神之奥皆臻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376560_comment'></div>阴伏阳升。虽鳞介之微必动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376560_comment'></div>道既如此。人焉忽诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376560_comment'></div>伏惟相公持重器以为霖。负英才而坐幄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376560_comment'></div>传丹青于直道。扇炉冶于至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376560_comment'></div>致一物之无遗。使万方之有赖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376560_comment'></div>某顾惟琐陋。获忝钧镕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376560_comment'></div>既契之于无私。固施之于不报。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376560_comment'></div>岂宜遽赍感激。窃拜门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376560_comment'></div>但以事出非常。恩从特异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376560_comment'></div>若不披于丹赤。终有负于神明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376560_comment'></div>伏惟俯降尊严。暂垂听察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376560_comment'></div>某才非敏干。性本颛愚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376560_comment'></div>自从振迹春闱。投身宦路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376560_comment'></div>徒绵岁月。莫致飞驰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376560_comment'></div>却则穷途。前皆散地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376560_comment'></div>是亦用之则未为国士。舍之则盖类腐儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376560_comment'></div>因自揣循。每加退缩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376560_comment'></div>然而窃念古人不远。贤路非遥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376560_comment'></div>皇朝自科擢英髦。爵升品秩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376560_comment'></div>其或来从草泽。生匪簪裾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376560_comment'></div>亦常列入清途。参为盛观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376560_comment'></div>所以益持<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376560", 1376560, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>孤孑</span>。尤切兢修。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376560_comment'></div>节励松筠。心倾葵藿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376560_comment'></div>常注目于烟霄之上。每驰魂于省闼之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376560_comment'></div>逮夫元鬓彫空。壮心折尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376560_comment'></div>曾无影响。空极瞻攀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376560_comment'></div>岂期相公才揭权衡。便垂采掇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376560_comment'></div>俾遭逢于圣日。令允惬于平生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376560_comment'></div>所谓材并得宜。物无遗性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376560_comment'></div>信造化之功不及。岂推迁之令能侔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376560_comment'></div>义贯古今。恩逾卵翼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376560_comment'></div>况相公峻于埏埴。切彼弼谐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376560_comment'></div>当今士号如林。朝称不乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376560_comment'></div>足得廓其公选。择以良才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376560_comment'></div>而某己怀耕钓之心。近闭云林之迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376560_comment'></div>设令漏网。未曰遗贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376560_comment'></div>是何特达开怀。周旋轸念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376560_comment'></div>青山在目。方将鱼鸟以同归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376560_comment'></div>鸿渥连天。忽历烟霞而曲被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376560_comment'></div>从杏坛之旧籍。践兰署之清资。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376560_comment'></div>岂是常情。谅非小事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376560_comment'></div>伏自荣叨幞被。幸窃含香。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376560_comment'></div>未尝一夕暂安。片时不感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376560_comment'></div>常若千钧之在顶。每将孤剑以誓诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376560_comment'></div>但以有地受恩。无门沥恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376560_comment'></div>只眄高车而激切。空持<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1376560", 1376560, "Clauses/93/Comments/0")'>敝帚</span>以屏营。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376560_comment'></div>泪则汍澜。心唯恐悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376560_comment'></div>瞻风拜赐。对景怀仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376560_comment'></div>涸彼言泉。固申陈而未尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376560_comment'></div>托于笔札。岂写载以能周。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376560_comment'></div>攀谢兢惶。罔知所措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376560_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_52_1376560_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=875&endYear=875')">875年</a>　干谒郑諴，约代郑諴上书郑畋。作品：《代郑郎中上兴道郑相启？》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376559' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376559' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376559?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑郎中上兴道郑相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（875年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376559")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376559_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376559'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376559'>伏念石甫受知于途中。鬷蔑申言于堂下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376559_comment'></div>既情非曩旧。复地隔尊卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376559_comment'></div>尚能感动至公。遭逢殊礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376559_comment'></div>而某神资所向。天受其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376559_comment'></div>获旷代之因依。得千年之幸会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376559_comment'></div>岂可永缄丹赤。上负陶钧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376559_comment'></div>伏惟相公特降恩慈。俯垂恻隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376559_comment'></div>昔年羽化。曾陪莺谷之春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376559_comment'></div>今日云飞。俄隔凤池之路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376559_comment'></div>信<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>鹤鸡</span>之果异。谅<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>牛骥</span>之终悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376559_comment'></div>徒增倚玉之荣。几积续貂之愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376559_comment'></div>况相公负英才而作砺。持硕望以登庸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376559_comment'></div>始者四海倾心。一人侧席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376559_comment'></div>朝闻坐幄。暮见飞霖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376559_comment'></div>扇浇薄为淳风。激<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>谗邪</span>归直道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376559_comment'></div>均施<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>炉冶</span>。高揭权衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376559_comment'></div>使铅汞之不参。令锱铢之各等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376559_comment'></div>故得方圆任器。高下随宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376559_comment'></div>黜陟无偏。贤愚有序。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376559_comment'></div>某早甘退迹。忽喜逢时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376559_comment'></div>遽从学省之前衔。爰践兰宫之峻级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376559_comment'></div>己为尘忝。诚合揣循。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376559_comment'></div>窃思顷年九陌秋天。都堂雪夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376559_comment'></div>常容披雾。每许参琼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376559_comment'></div>逮夫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/48/Comments/0")'>片玉</span>升科。兼金列榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376559_comment'></div>虽登龙群彦。同戴邱山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376559_comment'></div>而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_26_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/52/Comments/0")'>附凤</span>一心。偏投胶漆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376559_comment'></div>既以宗盟属意。仍从知旧留情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376559_comment'></div>重謺依投。绸缪奖录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376559_comment'></div>遂使庆钟末路。福逮今辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376559_comment'></div>既预门墙。仍从<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>埏埴</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376559_comment'></div>宛得御车之便。无烦拥彗之劳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376559_comment'></div>但以某<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1376559", 1376559, "Clauses/64/Comments/0")'>弱羽</span>难高。么弦易断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376559_comment'></div>始自筮仕。及于登朝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376559_comment'></div>未尝暂识清途。略游华贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376559_comment'></div>亦人地之所拘限。何穷通之切咨嗟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376559_comment'></div>洎夫郢俗褰帷。穰城建隼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376559_comment'></div>连叨竹使。尤愧棠阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376559_comment'></div>虽皂盖红旌。别过素望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376559_comment'></div>而霜台粉署。终系丹心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376559_comment'></div>今则荣窃握兰。幸当襆被。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376559_comment'></div>冯唐历践。诚知戴白之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376559_comment'></div>贡禹栖迟。且有弹冠之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376559_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1376559_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8ba21a54ef6d42e2aac67ec04a2693dc_label'><a id='poem_title_47365_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47365'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47365'>谁识在官意，开门树色间。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47365'>寻幽频宿寺，乞假拟归山。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47365'>半白侵吟鬓，微红见药颜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47365'>不知琴月夜<span class='inlineComment2'>（一作今夜月）</span>，几客得同闲。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47365_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47365'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47365_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376554' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376554' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376554?labeling=true' class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376554'>昨辄以近试赋轻黩门墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376554_comment'></div>韵匪掷金。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376554_comment'></div>理宜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>诮石</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376554_comment'></div>岂期转祸为福。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376554_comment'></div>以寸获长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376554_comment'></div>户部郑郎中伏话员外仁恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376554_comment'></div>大赐奖录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376554_comment'></div>拜聆嘉耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376554_comment'></div>跪对吉辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376554_comment'></div>感惕兢惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376554_comment'></div>进退失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376554_comment'></div>实以从古干时之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376554_comment'></div>至今取第之由。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376554_comment'></div>莫不路邈鳌头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376554_comment'></div>程悬骥尾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376554_comment'></div>苟非先鸣汲引。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376554_comment'></div>哲匠发挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376554_comment'></div>纵或自强。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376554_comment'></div>行将安适。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376554_comment'></div>伏以员外<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>断籯</span>积学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376554_comment'></div>计斗负才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376554_comment'></div>龟镜词林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376554_comment'></div>梯航陆海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376554_comment'></div>是故门骈<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>郑市</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376554_comment'></div>俗垫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>郭巾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376554_comment'></div>争俟栽培。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376554_comment'></div>互希丹饰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376554_comment'></div>而滔<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/27/Comments/0")'>牛涔</span>浅狭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376554_comment'></div>燕戏微茫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376554_comment'></div>岂合攀投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376554_comment'></div>徒为激切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376554_comment'></div>员外燕中市骏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376554_comment'></div>稷下馆人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376554_comment'></div>皆使有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376554_comment'></div>不言无取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376554_comment'></div>猥流厚旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376554_comment'></div>曲降隆私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376554_comment'></div>滔是敢引事推言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376554_comment'></div>徵文借喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376554_comment'></div>且杰如韩信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376554_comment'></div>未归汉祖以谁知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376554_comment'></div>美若西施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376554_comment'></div>不入吴宫而孰验。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376554_comment'></div>所以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>蛰剑</span>而凌虚吐耀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376554_comment'></div>焦桐而骇耳飞声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376554_comment'></div>然后感动良知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376554_comment'></div>遭逢至鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376554_comment'></div>事虽小异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376554_comment'></div>理或大同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376554_comment'></div>伏惟稍降尊严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376554_comment'></div>俯垂恻隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376554_comment'></div>如滔昧为贡士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376554_comment'></div>浅作丈夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376554_comment'></div>方今不右武功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376554_comment'></div>大先文教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376554_comment'></div>矫辞人于莺谷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376554_comment'></div>钥宗伯于龙门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376554_comment'></div>其有负马之文华。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376554_comment'></div>韫颜之德行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376554_comment'></div>或栖栖以至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376554_comment'></div>或岳岳而来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376554_comment'></div>未尝不坐驰日下之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376554_comment'></div>立贮彀中之望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376554_comment'></div>是何谢兹振发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376554_comment'></div>而处彼幽沉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376554_comment'></div>频年厕角逐之场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376554_comment'></div>众口蔑殊尤之誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376554_comment'></div>齐国<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_67_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>彗秃</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376554_comment'></div>荆山眼枯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376554_comment'></div>渐觉途穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376554_comment'></div>虚云舌在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376554_comment'></div>岂可坚期<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_71_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/71/Comments/0")'>御李</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376554_comment'></div>确慕依刘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376554_comment'></div>志空切于投林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376554_comment'></div>丑难逃于测管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376554_comment'></div>伏惟员外<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_75_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/75/Comments/0")'>魏车委照</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376554_comment'></div>轩匣扬光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376554_comment'></div>傥怜其刻意探幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376554_comment'></div>焦心体物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376554_comment'></div>则虽异于披沙之说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376554_comment'></div>然略几于架屋之谭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376554_comment'></div>许列<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_81_1376554", 1376554, "Clauses/81/Comments/0")'>书筠</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376554_comment'></div>令参撰杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376554_comment'></div>今者或因荐士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376554_comment'></div>敢乞编名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376554_comment'></div>所希从数仞墙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376554_comment'></div>伴二三子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376554_comment'></div>增辉琐质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376554_comment'></div>擅价主人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376554_comment'></div>皆由一顾之仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376554_comment'></div>翘伫百金之诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376554_comment'></div>含毫汗下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376554_comment'></div>伏纸魂惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376554_comment'></div>非切觊觎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376554_comment'></div>所忧诛戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376554_comment'></div>叨越干犯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376554_comment'></div>下情无任战惧屏营之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_96_1376554_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=876&endYear=876')">876年</a>　有启与郑諴。作品：《刑部郑郞中启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《第二启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376550' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376550' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376550'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376550'>滔学异生知。才非夙搆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376550_comment'></div>虽叨进取。莫俟遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376550_comment'></div>郎中模楷词林。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376550", 1376550, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>梯航</span>名路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376550_comment'></div>每虑或遗于片善。常忧不采于一言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376550_comment'></div>比者伏蒙曲念虚芜。荣流咳唾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376550_comment'></div>诲以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1376550", 1376550, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>磨铅</span>未至。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1376550", 1376550, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>刻楮</span>非工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376550_comment'></div>冥心于雪夜花朝。空徵六义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376550_comment'></div>属意于国风王泽。罔造二南。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376550_comment'></div>将令罢课缘情。回从体物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376550_comment'></div>伏自穰城去骑。灞岸归蹄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376550_comment'></div>时迈青阳。景融朱火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376550_comment'></div>于是凝神扣寂。闭迹探幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376550_comment'></div>盖希副非次之恩知。非敢切平生之志业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376550_comment'></div>昨者伏遇南宫拜命。北阙朝天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376550_comment'></div>岂惟上贺于高翔。仍喜旁陈其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1376550", 1376550, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>末艺</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376550_comment'></div>永期指教。毕愿<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376550", 1376550, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>攀依</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376550_comment'></div>而以浅近怀惭。雕镌积愧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376550_comment'></div>前而复却。决以还疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376550_comment'></div>空眷恋于门墙。竟迟回于书幕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376550_comment'></div>今则难逃皎镜。须诣平衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376550_comment'></div>冀分妍丑之姿。式定重轻之品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376550_comment'></div>伏惟特固朝暾之旨。俯怜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_21_1376550", 1376550, "Clauses/43/Comments/0")'>夕死</span>之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376550_comment'></div>荐赐发言。重将辨惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376550_comment'></div>临风股慄。伏纸心忡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376550_comment'></div>倾写依投。不任激切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376550_comment'></div>试赋一轴。谨诣宅祗候陈献。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376550_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1376550_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_1376561' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376561?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代郑郎中上令狐相启</a><span class='authorDate'>（876年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span id='poem_title_1376561_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376561'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376561'>某今月四日转授刑部郎中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376561_comment'></div>伏蒙相公仁恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376561_comment'></div>特赐<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376561", 1376561, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>宠诲</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376561_comment'></div>事从非次。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376561_comment'></div>言异常伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376561_comment'></div>感激兢惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376561_comment'></div>进退失措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376561_comment'></div>伏以某材非可采。<div id='poem_sentence_9_1376561_comment'></div>树为梯级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376561_comment'></div>才荣地部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376561_comment'></div>复陟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376561", 1376561, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>秋曹</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376561_comment'></div>持鹪鹩决起之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376561_comment'></div>到鸑鷟曾栖之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376561_comment'></div>相公怜其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376561", 1376561, "Clauses/15/Comments/0")'>拙滞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376561_comment'></div>忽此<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_22_1376561_comment'></div>向来一字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376561_comment'></div>爰垂鲁史之褒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376561_comment'></div>义极生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376561_comment'></div>彩逾丹雘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376561_comment'></div>拜窥垂露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376561_comment'></div>跪捧隆私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376561_comment'></div>汗浃背流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376561_comment'></div>泪盈眦下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376561_comment'></div>未知顺风弱力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376561_comment'></div><span class='link' id='poem_sentence_33_1376561_comment'></div>何报千钧之重意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376561_comment'></div>唯谨缄于箧笥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376561_comment'></div>常誇向于缙绅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376561_comment'></div>为官路之遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376561_comment'></div>作仕流之卓异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376561_comment'></div>攀谢恳切。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376561_comment'></div>不任下情。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1376561_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=876&endYear=876')">876年</a>　代陈蠲撰文谢崔沆。作品：《代陈蠲谢崔侍郞启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376562' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376562' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376562?labeling=true' target='_blank'>代陈蠲谢崔侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（876年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376562")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376562_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376562'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376562'>某启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376562_comment'></div>户部郑郎中伏话郑隐先辈专传侍郎尊旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376562_comment'></div>伏蒙于新除永乐侍郎处特赐荐论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376562_comment'></div>跪对吉辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376562_comment'></div>拜聆嘉耗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376562_comment'></div>感激兢悚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376562_comment'></div>罔知所容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376562_comment'></div>某词学<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376562", 1376562, "Clauses/7/Comments/0")'>疏芜</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376562_comment'></div>进取乖拙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376562_comment'></div>一叨贡士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376562_comment'></div>累黜名场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376562_comment'></div>足间之刖处纵横。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376562_comment'></div>额上之点痕重謺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376562_comment'></div>今春伏遇侍郎精求俊彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376562_comment'></div>历选滞遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376562_comment'></div>某又名碍龙头。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376562_comment'></div>迹乖豹变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376562_comment'></div>都由薄命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376562_comment'></div>翻负至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376562_comment'></div>以此<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376562", 1376562, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>怔忪</span>莫宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376562_comment'></div>惶惑无已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376562_comment'></div>在良时而自失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376562_comment'></div>于异日以何归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376562_comment'></div>谓一生而便可甘心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376562_comment'></div>叹二纪而徒劳苦节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376562_comment'></div>岂料侍郎坚垂记录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376562_comment'></div>确赐恤伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376562_comment'></div>令后人而副取前心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376562_comment'></div>指陋质而说为遗恨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376562_comment'></div>将使蔡经之骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376562_comment'></div>终系仙家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376562_comment'></div>士燮之魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376562_comment'></div>却还人世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376562_comment'></div>盖施阴德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376562_comment'></div>岂止阳功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376562_comment'></div>喜极翻惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376562_comment'></div>感深唯泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376562_comment'></div>明年春色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376562_comment'></div>致身虽出于他门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376562_comment'></div>今日恩光。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376562_comment'></div>碎首须归于旧地。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1376562_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=877&endYear=877')">877年2月</a>　应试落第，东归前撰文与崔沆。作品：《崔右丞启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《第二启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376571' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376571' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376571'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376571'>滔献赋命奇。食贫计尽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376571_comment'></div>难安<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1376571", 1376571, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>桂玉</span>。须逐萍蓬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376571_comment'></div>伏念灞浐行尘。周秦去路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376571_comment'></div>平言南北。犹悄神魂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376571_comment'></div>况今攀托门墙。依凭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1376571", 1376571, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>奖顾</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376571_comment'></div>以坑谷苍黄之态。戴邱山岌嶪之恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376571_comment'></div>得不欲别还留。将行复却。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376571_comment'></div>丹诚聚血。双泪流珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376571_comment'></div>矧当杏苑烟晴。柳沟风暖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376571_comment'></div>陌上而群英得意。尘中而衰发伤离。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376571_comment'></div>设令勇若荆轲。固亦恸如阮籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376571_comment'></div>伏以右丞宏施阴德。浚哲仁心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376571_comment'></div>傥或<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376571", 1376571, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>荑枯</span>肉骨之未忘。则胶柱刻舟而敢怠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376571_comment'></div>宁言今日。唯惕将来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376571_comment'></div>迟回数仞之墙边。移时忍去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376571_comment'></div>怆恨九重之城外。举策何之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376571_comment'></div>感恋屏营。罔知攸处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376571_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1376571_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: id='poem_title_47327_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47327'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47327'>背将踪迹向京师，出在先春入后时。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47327'>落日灞桥飞雪里，已闻南院有看期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47327_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence'
