class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=891&endYear=895')">891-895年</a>，52-56岁</div><div id='97fc8f6974e24ad19dd4bf2522ec9cc5' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=891&endYear=891')">891年</a>　到长安备举，有文与杨赞禹，谢其援引。作品：《与杨状头书》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《与杨状头赞图启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376545' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376545' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376545?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与杨状头书</a><span class='authorDate'>（891年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376545")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376545_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376545'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376545'>谨献书状元先辈。圣人之道没。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376545_comment'></div>必假后贤以援之。故天将假后贤以援之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376545_comment'></div>必先否其人之数。而后克亨其道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376545_comment'></div>苟知厥理。繇是得而言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376545_comment'></div>且咸通乾符之贡士。其有德行文学人地如先辈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376545_comment'></div>而在举场。则其举罕再。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376545_comment'></div>而先辈在举场逮二十年。何哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376545_comment'></div>是知天否先辈当年之数。以亨今日之道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376545_comment'></div>假于春官天官之网。首冠群彦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376545_comment'></div>基我中兴。使天下之人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376545_comment'></div>翕然向风。奔走慕义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376545_comment'></div>以偃干戈。岂不然乎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376545_comment'></div>今俾天下之人。奔走瞻之为龙门管钥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376545_comment'></div>宗伯之处士也。莫不俟我之启。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376545_comment'></div>某顷者频试于小宗伯。姓名罔为人之所闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376545_comment'></div>然多受知于前辈。故安州郑郎中江陵蒋校书谓所业赋偶公道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376545_comment'></div>必为宗师之荐。宗伯之求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376545_comment'></div>某佩斯言十有五年矣。幸蜀之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376545_comment'></div>东蛰闽越。洎前年榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376545_comment'></div>伏睹先辈荣登。逮王先辈希龙之还。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376545_comment'></div>敬话先辈之道。某熟得而知勉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376545_comment'></div>某提携所业。直扣门仞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376545_comment'></div>昨某之来也。朝及京师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376545_comment'></div>暮期刺谒。今幸于此遽获贽投。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376545_comment'></div>果蒙先辈逾涯越等。加之赏录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376545_comment'></div>更许荐拔。充宗伯之所求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376545_comment'></div>则二贤之言斯验矣。若某则已登选于今日也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376545_comment'></div>某草泽单寒。无门报德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376545_comment'></div>且世之感恩谢知。罔不率以杀身为之辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376545_comment'></div>夫杀身之期。是待知己于患难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376545_comment'></div>某今感先辈之恩知。谨唯铭刻肌骨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376545_comment'></div>故献书于座右以陈露之。伏惟始终怜察焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376545_comment'></div>不宣。某再拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376545_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_33_1376545_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376558' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376558' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376558?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与杨状头赞图启</a><span class='authorDate'>（891年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376558")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376558_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376558'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376558'>滔骤持末学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376558_comment'></div>遽窃殊知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376558_comment'></div>伏自豫章数旬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376558_comment'></div>湓浦一路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376558_comment'></div>扃旅舍而夜唯假寐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376558_comment'></div>逐征帆而日但沾衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376558_comment'></div>盖以虔戴遭逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376558_comment'></div>仰思情旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376558_comment'></div>先辈主中兴之文学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376558_comment'></div>作来者之蓍龟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376558_comment'></div>伏蒙采滔所业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376558_comment'></div>异于等伦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376558_comment'></div>悯滔所举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376558_comment'></div>困于曩昔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376558_comment'></div>大张金口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376558_comment'></div>精发瑶函。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376558_comment'></div>且<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_16_1376558", 1376558, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>午火</span>烧空。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376558_comment'></div>一阴司月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376558_comment'></div>面泉石或病乎炎毒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376558_comment'></div>处城池而奈彼郁蒸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376558_comment'></div>况土风则竹屋玲珑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376558_comment'></div>烟水则叶舟荡漾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376558_comment'></div>才晓而乌光赫透。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376558_comment'></div>欲风而鱼沫腥飘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376558_comment'></div>虽付于醴酒酕醄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376558_comment'></div>或亡坏混。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376558_comment'></div>又属其羽书重謺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376558_comment'></div>时触高明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376558_comment'></div>诚知不乏馀波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376558_comment'></div>争奈罕闻暇日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376558_comment'></div>岂可更抽秘思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376558_comment'></div>别运真踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376558_comment'></div>每摛一幅之霞笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376558_comment'></div>咸滴千痕之雨汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376558_comment'></div>虽才高倚马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376558_comment'></div>曾无起草之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376558_comment'></div>而字悉如蝇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376558_comment'></div>几若生胝之笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376558_comment'></div>未知单贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376558_comment'></div>何补生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376558_comment'></div>赍行而便自金丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376558_comment'></div>举步而即升云汉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376558_comment'></div>矧复公言私论。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376558_comment'></div>要诀神方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376558_comment'></div>一一指踪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376558_comment'></div>头头传授。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376558_comment'></div>将克周于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_46_1376558", 1376558, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>顶踵</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376558_comment'></div>俾无失于毫釐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376558_comment'></div>以此推恩而前古所稀。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376558_comment'></div>以此行道而方今谁比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376558_comment'></div>士林名路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376558_comment'></div>一朝有知己如斯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376558_comment'></div>白日青天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376558_comment'></div>万世唯子孙为誓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376558_comment'></div>下情无任感恩泣泪悚谢之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_54_1376558_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=891&endYear=891')">891年</a>　到长安备举，有文与裴贽。作品：《与裴侍郎启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376576' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376576' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376576?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与裴侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（891年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376576")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376576_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376576'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376576'>滔伏念荐孟明则子桑所能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376576_comment'></div>免叔向匪祁奚莫议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376576_comment'></div>推言及是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376576_comment'></div>沥恳为宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376576_comment'></div>上渎清隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376576_comment'></div>敢希容听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376576_comment'></div>伏惟侍郎中丞顷持文柄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376576_comment'></div>大阐至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376576_comment'></div>垂为圣代之准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376576_comment'></div>悬作贡闱之日月。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376576_comment'></div>滔为后无私之两榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376576_comment'></div>遂乖必字于十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376576_comment'></div>伏蒙侍郎中丞曲赐悯伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376576_comment'></div>直加赏录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376576_comment'></div>连岁荐论琐质。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376576_comment'></div>倾极重言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376576_comment'></div>而以弱植难培。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376576_comment'></div>么弦易断。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376576_comment'></div>且惊负累。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376576_comment'></div>空费生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376576_comment'></div>既而不罪龙钟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376576_comment'></div>愈隆恩遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376576_comment'></div>昨者面容<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376576", 1376576, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>跪履</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376576_comment'></div>亲俾窥天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376576_comment'></div>仍加琢玉之品题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376576_comment'></div>更启如金之然诺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376576_comment'></div>便于此日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376576_comment'></div>上翥重霄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376576_comment'></div>今则已除主文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376576_comment'></div>只祈阴德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376576_comment'></div>延颈于沟隍之底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376576_comment'></div>瞻恩于邱岳之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376576_comment'></div>虽龟龙不瑞于匹夫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376576_comment'></div>而犬马合由于本主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376576_comment'></div>沾巾堕睫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376576_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1376576", 1376576, "Clauses/35/Comments/0")'>沥胆披肝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376576_comment'></div>不在他门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376576_comment'></div>誓于死节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376576_comment'></div>下情无任攀托依投恳悃之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_38_1376576_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=892&endYear=894')">892-894年</a>　应试、干谒。作品：《翰林薛舍人启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《薛舍人启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《贺杨侍郎启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《和陈先辈陪陆舍人春日游曲江》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《投翰长赵侍郎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《赵起居启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376575' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376575' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376575?labeling=true' target='_blank'>翰林薛舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（892年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376575")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376575_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376575'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376575'>滔伏以十一日才除<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376575", 1376575, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>主文</span>。旋沥情恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376575_comment'></div>罪责则可言于躁切。悯伤则宜恕于单危。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376575_comment'></div>非不三省九思。沉吟笺管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376575_comment'></div>而以途穷日暮。恐惧风波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376575_comment'></div>亦犹抱沉痾者悉将虔告于神医。怀至痛者无不上呼于穹碧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376575_comment'></div>伏以学士舍人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1376575", 1376575, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>轩铜</span>照胆。蜀秤悬心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376575_comment'></div>仰惟<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1376575", 1376575, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>烛临</span>。当极幽奥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376575_comment'></div>且夫礼司取士。寒进升名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376575_comment'></div>若无哲匠以斲成。未有良时而自致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376575_comment'></div>不然者。则安得权悬至鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376575_comment'></div>代有遗人。伏惟学士舍人标表士林。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376575_comment'></div>梯航陆海。凡言进取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376575_comment'></div>须自门墙。今以文柄有归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376575_comment'></div>至公宏播。则精力固同于造化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376575_comment'></div>嘉言乃作于蓍龟。而滔折角有年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376575_comment'></div>交锋无托。羽毛零落。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376575_comment'></div>鬐鬣摧残。若不自学士舍人推恩极山岳之隆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376575_comment'></div>攘臂到沟隍之底。则还惭抱瓮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376575_comment'></div>难出戴盆。兼近者面获起居。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376575_comment'></div>亲承念录。哀滔昔年五随计吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376575_comment'></div>刖双足以全空。今复三历贡闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376575_comment'></div>救陆沉而未暇。许垂敏手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376575_comment'></div>拯上重霄。谨以誓向鬼神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376575_comment'></div>刻于肌骨。中兴教化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376575_comment'></div>一身免没于风尘。下国儿孙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376575_comment'></div>百世敢忘于厮隶。下情无任攀投恳悃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376575_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_26_1376575_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376578' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376578' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376578?labeling=true' target='_blank'>薛舍人启</a><span class='authorDate'>（892年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376578")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376578_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376578'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376578'>今月二十八日。张道古参军仰传仁恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376578_comment'></div>伏承舍人学士不以滔幽沉。荣赐论荐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376578_comment'></div>初疑梦寐。旋认生成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376578_comment'></div>不知所容。兢惶战悸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376578_comment'></div>伏以舍人学士半千膺数。全硕负才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376578_comment'></div>嘉名冠绝于九流。逸步翱翔于四户。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376578_comment'></div>顷者重于知己。避以文闱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376578_comment'></div>隆行望于圣贤。蓄基负于台鼎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376578_comment'></div>窃惟荐士。岂易其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376578_comment'></div>而滔踪迹蹉跎。艺能浅薄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376578_comment'></div>敢期宏造。遽及兹辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376578_comment'></div>金口开时。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1376578", 1376578, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>讲贯</span>则处其异等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376578_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376578", 1376578, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>瑶函</span>发处。推扬则寘彼极言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376578_comment'></div>事出殊常。荣非所望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376578_comment'></div>感深唯泣。喜过翻惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376578_comment'></div>不知微生。何酬厚遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376578_comment'></div>中兴教化。馀年获出于沟隍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376578_comment'></div>下国儿孙。累世敢忘于厮隶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376578_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1376578_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376577' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376577' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376577?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺杨侍郎启</a><span class='authorDate'>（893年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376577")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376577_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376577'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376577'>伏以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376577", 1376577, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>羲爻</span>不兆之文。何人复演。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376577_comment'></div>鲁史不褒之言。旷古谁称。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376577_comment'></div>厥理非遥。斯言可喻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376577_comment'></div>伏以侍郎荣司<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1376577", 1376577, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>文柄</span>。宏阐至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376577_comment'></div>历选滞遗。精求文行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376577_comment'></div>泉下则大臣有感。揭起销沉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376577_comment'></div>场中则寒族无差。酌平先后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376577_comment'></div>所以如滔者。曾干衡镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376577_comment'></div>经定否臧。若不蒙指向后人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376577_comment'></div>说为遗恨。则宰辅之为荐举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376577_comment'></div>帝王之作知音。而主且不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376577_comment'></div>人谁肯信。由是须作侍郎金口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376577_comment'></div>须自侍郎瑶函。今则论启无私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376577_comment'></div>恩加琐质。锡生成于此日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376577_comment'></div>迥分付于将来。早从握内以挤排。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376577_comment'></div>便是眼前之科第。然后念以渐临风水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376577_comment'></div>莫如蓬岛之音尘。俾拜云天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376577_comment'></div>亲吐兰言而诲谕。留心及是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376577_comment'></div>自古所希。莫不拳跼循涯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376577_comment'></div>阑干抹泣。质向神鬼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376577_comment'></div>誓于子孙。莺谷乘春。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376577_comment'></div>虽托他门而振羽。糜躯异日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376577_comment'></div>须归旧地以论恩。沥肝胆以无穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376577_comment'></div>寓笺毫而莫戴。下情无任感恩恳悃之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376577_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_24_1376577_comment'></div></div></div><div class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376570' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376570?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赵起居启</a><span class='authorDate'>（894年）</span><span id='poem_sentence_0_1376570'>滔今月二十日。辄以所业赋一轴陈献清严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376570_comment'></div>持腐草之造扶桑。鞭段之触骐骥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376570_comment'></div>所宜唾面。敢俟回眸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376570_comment'></div>伏以起居为八韵之咸韶。作九流之溟渤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376570_comment'></div>凡言进取。须自品题。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376570_comment'></div>而滔二纪飘零。三朝困辱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376570_comment'></div>若不仰投门馆。虔伫<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1376570", 1376570, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>发扬</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376570_comment'></div>则永携<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_1376570", 1376570, "Clauses/14/Comments/0")'>疑玉</span>以汍澜。长伴<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_8_1376570_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_1376570_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=895&endYear=895')">895年</a>　应礼部试。作品：《人文化天下赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《省试内出白鹿宣示百宫》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376533' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376533' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376533?labeling=true' target='_blank'>省试人文化天下赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以观彼人文以化天下为韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（895年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376533")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376533_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376533'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376533'>明彼今古。闻诸圣贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376533_comment'></div>易垂言而著在八卦。人有文而形于普天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376533_comment'></div>用以成章。既验斯风之肃穆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376533_comment'></div>瞩之于物。乃知厥德之昭宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376533_comment'></div>吾君秉此格言。恢乎至理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376533_comment'></div>以为文在天而苟可鉴。文在人而诚足视。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376533_comment'></div>在天则时变从之。在人则化成有以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376533_comment'></div>故体此以御宇。取兹而教人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376533_comment'></div>且文也。肇自河龟见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376533_comment'></div>洛书陈。道德故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376533_comment'></div>仁义新。出无为而入有象。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376533_comment'></div>齐父子而一君臣。既而上古遐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376533_comment'></div>中古迩。苟流播之如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376533_comment'></div>乃弛张而若彼。始则六十四位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376533_comment'></div>演自周王。旋则三百五篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376533_comment'></div>删于孔氏。故得有国之君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376533_comment'></div>准绳斯文。诗书礼乐以表里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376533_comment'></div>干戚俎豆以区分。莫不经天纬地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376533_comment'></div>髣髴氤氲。布彼寰瀛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376533_comment'></div>风行而草偃。被于亿兆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376533_comment'></div>玉洁而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376533", 1376533, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>兰薰</span>。然后铿作咸韶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376533_comment'></div>散为风雅。调畅动植。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376533_comment'></div>周通夷夏。车书得以合矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376533_comment'></div>贵贱与而同也。遂使九州四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376533_comment'></div>皆瞻黼黻于朝端。墨客词人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376533_comment'></div>交露锋铓于笔下。大哉人文之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376533_comment'></div>焕矣赫矣。可名可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376533_comment'></div>唯圣朝之所擅。岂悖德之能干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376533_comment'></div>推其时而时或异。论其道而道斯完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376533_comment'></div>故将垂百王而作范。岂惟充万国以咸欢者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376533_comment'></div>夫如是。则肩比三王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376533_comment'></div>威销五霸。宏彰驭马之成政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376533_comment'></div>克俾雕龙之擅价。彬彬乎哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376533_comment'></div>郁郁乎哉。有以见我唐之至化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376533_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1376533_comment'></div></div></div><div "poem_allusion_47363")'>玉颓</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_47363_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47363'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47363'>帝尧城里日衔杯，每倚嵇康到<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(2208, "poem_sentence_0_47363")'>玉颓</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47363'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_47363", 47363, "Clauses/2/Comments/0")'>桂苑</span>五更听榜后，蓬山二月看花开。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47363'>垂名<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_47363", 47363, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>入甲</span>成龙去，列姓如丁作鹤来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47363'>同戴大恩何处报，永言交道契<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(1470, "poem_sentence_3_47363")'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_47363", 47363, "Clauses/7/Comments/1")'>陈雷</span></span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47363_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47363'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47363_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=895&endYear=895')">895年2月</a>　昭宗令重试。作品：《曲直不相入赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《良弓献问赋》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376543' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376543' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376543?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御试曲直不相入赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（以题中曲直两字为韵）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（895年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376543")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376543_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376543'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376543'>曲也者。厥理惟何。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376543_comment'></div>直也者。其辞可属。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376543_comment'></div>一则见回邪之所自。一则非平正而不欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376543_comment'></div>故圣人立此格言。为乎懿躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376543_comment'></div>俾有家而有国。不与混同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376543_comment'></div>令自高而自卑。靡相<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1376543", 1376543, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>参触</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376543_comment'></div>至如木也。或表从绳之直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376543_comment'></div>或謺来巢之曲。虽则含烟带雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376543_comment'></div>共呈苍翠于岩间。而耸本盘根。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376543_comment'></div>各禀规模于山足。勿言同地而错杂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376543_comment'></div>固乃殊途而瞻瞩。所以方能中矩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376543_comment'></div>俟良匠之所知。劲不为轮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376543_comment'></div>信奇材而可录。莫不分彼邪正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376543_comment'></div>镇于时俗。且木之理兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376543_comment'></div>犹不差忒。人之道兮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376543_comment'></div>切在忠直。直也不可以曲从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376543_comment'></div>曲也不可以直饰。行于己而己有异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376543_comment'></div>施于人而人是测。由是屈原在楚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376543_comment'></div>餔其糟而不为。比干相殷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376543_comment'></div>剖其心而可得。顾惟忠谠之受性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376543_comment'></div>岂与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_20_1376543", 1376543, "Clauses/40/Comments/0")'>邪谀</span>而同域。其不相入也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376543_comment'></div>理苟如是。俗奚以惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376543_comment'></div>小人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376543", 1376543, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>曲媚</span>。或乘造次以得时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376543_comment'></div>君子<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_23_1376543", 1376543, "Clauses/46/Comments/0")'>直诚</span>。可仗英明而辅国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376543_comment'></div>今我后恢睿哲以御乾。澄圣心而立极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376543_comment'></div>恶似钩而在物。乐如弦而比德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376543_comment'></div>惟曲是斥。彰万乘之准绳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376543_comment'></div>惟直是求。示百王之楷式。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376543_comment'></div>微臣之获咏歌。敢不佩之于取则。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376543_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_29_1376543_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1376544' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376544' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376544?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御试良弓献问赋<span class='inlineComment2'>（取五声字次第用各双声为赋格）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（895年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376544")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376544_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376544'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376544'>文皇帝以精求要义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376544_comment'></div>下访良弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376544_comment'></div>以木心之邪正既别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376544_comment'></div>将理道之比方乃同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376544_comment'></div>木若有邪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376544_comment'></div>奚副准绳之一一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376544_comment'></div>理如无苟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376544_comment'></div>必资国祚之崇崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376544_comment'></div>斯盖体元立制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376544_comment'></div>启圣乘乾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376544_comment'></div>与禹汤而接轸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376544_comment'></div>将尧舜以差肩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376544_comment'></div>睹于物也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376544_comment'></div>必有诚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376544_comment'></div>言念为弓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376544_comment'></div>尚穷元于脉理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376544_comment'></div>岂于有国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376544_comment'></div>不注意于英贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376544_comment'></div>否则何以宏丕图于赫赫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376544_comment'></div>垂宝祚于绵绵者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376544_comment'></div>则知黄帝造舟车之旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376544_comment'></div>其难为比。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376544_comment'></div>周武倒干戈之文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376544_comment'></div>殊不称美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376544_comment'></div>观草木而尚此烛幽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376544_comment'></div>统寰区而足彰致理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376544_comment'></div>遂使度木抡材之子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376544_comment'></div>每自依依。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376544_comment'></div>献可替否之臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376544_comment'></div>曾非唯唯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376544_comment'></div>今吾皇播声教以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1376544", 1376544, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>锵洋</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376544_comment'></div>浚恩波而浩汗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376544_comment'></div>乾坤与之而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_32_1376544", 1376544, "Clauses/32/Comments/0")'>合德</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376544_comment'></div>夷夏有之而一贯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376544_comment'></div>斯弓不制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376544_comment'></div>洞其理以明明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376544_comment'></div>斯问克兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376544_comment'></div>露其言而粲粲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376544_comment'></div>儒有生在江岭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376544_comment'></div>来趋辇毂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376544_comment'></div>波涛久慕于化鲲兮<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。</div><div id='poem_sentence_40_1376544_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1376544'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_40_1376544_0'>⑴ 谨按洪迈容斋四笔此赋有五声后阙入声一韵</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1376544_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=895&endYear=895')">895年2月</a>　黄滔又及第，有诗。作品：《御试》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《成名后呈同年》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_47473' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47473' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47473?labeling=true' target='_blank'>御试二首<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>①</sup><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（895年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47473")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47473_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_47473_0'>① 昭宗乾宁二年，崔凝考定进士张贻宪等二十五人。复命所司覆试，内出四题，乃曲直不相入赋、良弓献问赋、询于刍荛诗、品物咸熙诗。赵观文、程晏、崔赏、崔仁宝等四人，并卢瞻、韦说、封渭、韦希震、张蠙、黄滔、卢鼎、王贞白、沈崧、陈晓、李龟祯等十一人，并与及第。其张贻宪、孙溥、李光序、李枢、李途等五人，且令落下，许后再举。其崔砺、苏楷、杜承昭、郑稼等四人，不令再举。内一人卢赓称疾不至，宣令舁入。又云华阴省亲，其父渥进状乞落下，故就试止二十四人也。</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47473'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47473'>已表隋珠各自携，更从琼殿立丹梯。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47473_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47473'>九华灯作三条烛，万乘君悬四首题。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47473_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47473'>灵凤敢期翻雪羽，洞箫应或讽金闺。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47473_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47473'>明朝莫惜场场醉，青桂新香有紫泥。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47473_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47473'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47473_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_47474' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47474' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47474?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（895年2月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47474_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47474'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47474'>六曹三省列簪裾，丹诏宣来试士初。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47474'>不是玉皇疑羽客，要教金榜带天书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47474'>词臣假寐题黄绢，宫女敲铜奏<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_47474", 47474, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>子虚</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47474'>御目四篇酬九百，敢从灯下略踌躇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47474_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47474'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47474_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_47506' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47506' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47506?labeling=true' target='_blank'>成名后呈同年</a><span class='authorDate'>（895年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47506")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_47506_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47506'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47506'>业诗攻赋荐乡书，二纪如鸿历九衢。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47506'>待得至公搜草泽，如从平陆到蓬壶。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47506'>虽惭<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_47506", 47506, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>锦鲤</span>成穿额，忝获骊龙不寐珠。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47506'>蒙楚数疑休下泣，师刘大喝已为卢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47506'>人间灰管供红杏，天上烟花应白榆。<div id='poem_sentence_4_47506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_47506'>一字连镳巡甲族，千般唱罚赏皇都。<div id='poem_sentence_5_47506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_47506'>名推颜柳题金塔，饮自燕秦索<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_47506", 47506, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>玉姝</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_47506_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_47506'>退愧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_47506", 47506, target='_blank'>南海韦尚书启</a><span class='authorDate'>（873年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376552")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376552_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376552'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376552'>滔伏念高为碧落。讵侧管以能窥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376552_comment'></div>深作沧溟。固持蠡而莫测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376552_comment'></div>焉可爰赍<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>琐智</span>。直杖小才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376552_comment'></div>叙昴宿之钟萧。述尼山之降孔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376552_comment'></div>既将越礼。诚可加刑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376552_comment'></div>然则有旷代之遭逢。获千年之际会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376552_comment'></div>设若旁扃辨囿。内遏言泉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376552_comment'></div>不惟上负于良时。抑亦下辜于卑志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376552_comment'></div>是致斋身搦管。沐发<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/17/Comments/0")'>裁辞</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376552_comment'></div>伏惟尚书象外三山。人间<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/19/Comments/0")'>七宝</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376552_comment'></div>体天地方圆之制。法阴阳升伏之机。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376552_comment'></div>自从见作<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>人龙</span>。翔为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_11_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/23/Comments/0")'>鸟凤</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376552_comment'></div>腾辉瑞牒。流庆皇家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376552_comment'></div>文章则游夏固迁。事业则伊皋周召。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376552_comment'></div>飞扬天上。践履朝端。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376552_comment'></div>且自古六官所重。莫先于吏部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376552_comment'></div>逮今贰职所难。无出于侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376552_comment'></div>而尚书五陟东西。两司铨管。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376552_comment'></div>矧复品量庶汇。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_18_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>选度</span>群材。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376552_comment'></div>载万乘之安危。系四方之休戚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376552_comment'></div>晋魏则大难斯地。国朝尤不易其人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376552_comment'></div>历数除书。少闻再命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376552_comment'></div>朝廷不欲止于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/44/Comments/0")'>鸳省</span>。便入凤池。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376552_comment'></div>须加分阃之尊。用饰作霖之盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376552_comment'></div>特以番禺巨壤。南越名区。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376552_comment'></div>外控蛮陬。旁通番货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376552_comment'></div>昔者石门酌泉之事。合浦还珠之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376552_comment'></div>日月<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/54/Comments/0")'>迁绵</span>。<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_27_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/55/Comments/0")'>规程</span>革易。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376552_comment'></div>以尚书励辞玉留钱之节。执投香载土之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376552_comment'></div>用将揭二贤廉洁之波。新五岭崎岖之俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376552_comment'></div>俾以佩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_30_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>豹韬</span>而直下。建龙节以遐征。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376552_comment'></div>非止镇临。且申龟镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376552_comment'></div>昭然足验。俨若可观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376552_comment'></div>然后飞驿骑以徵黄。降鹄书而命说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376552_comment'></div>恢张帝道。陶冶生灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376552_comment'></div>所以知高祖<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_35_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/70/Comments/0")'>创基</span>。太宗纂业。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376552_comment'></div>更得无疆之祚。仍归有截之风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376552_comment'></div>何以言之。伏以尚书万顷包含。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376552_comment'></div>千寻峭拔。膺岳峻河清之数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376552_comment'></div>切饮冰食檗之诚。识洞古今。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376552_comment'></div>居无喜愠。将以锵履声而朝紫殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376552_comment'></div>扩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/82/Comments/0")'>心秤</span>而启<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_41_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/82/Comments/1")'>洪钧</span>。自然道臻于尧舜羲轩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376552_comment'></div>时复于禹汤文武。百蛮向化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376552_comment'></div>万国归心。虽在愚蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376552_comment'></div>亦能辨识。而滔器同魏瓠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376552_comment'></div>凡若庄樗。握无蛇口之珍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376552_comment'></div>额有鱼身之点。今者遽持幽贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376552_comment'></div>获觐旌幢。兢营方忝于拂尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376552_comment'></div>奖遇旋叨于荐赋。且凡<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_48_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/97/Comments/0")'>开场</span>试士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376552_comment'></div>就铺属词。从物外之课虚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376552_comment'></div>向灯前以应限。纵若仲宣阁群公之笔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376552_comment'></div>长卿量陈后之金。空有所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376552_comment'></div>或闻未至。况滔虽勤篆刻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376552_comment'></div>且昧精奇。张平子固合陋都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376552_comment'></div>陆士衡所宜抚掌。宁期尚书亲回严重。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376552_comment'></div>庭赐褒称。变泥沙为丹雘之姿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376552_comment'></div>植<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_56_1376552", 1376552, "Clauses/112/Comments/0")'>菅蒯</span>作芝兰之秀。鲁史骤荣于一字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376552_comment'></div>晋庭俄采于片言。超越寻常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376552_comment'></div>震惊流辈。况方今武功草偃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376552_comment'></div>文教风行。计奔岁贡于九州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376552_comment'></div>榜擢词人于都省。至如生于草泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376552_comment'></div>来自沟塍。或能中甲乙求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376552_comment'></div>登殊尤选。盖止于同人延誉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376552_comment'></div>先达吹嘘。未尝有圣日名侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376552_comment'></div>大朝重德。面开金口。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376552_comment'></div>首借丹梯。以此推言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376552_comment'></div>便宜自贺。瑶枝玉干。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376552_comment'></div>虚扃皓月之中。羽驾云装。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376552_comment'></div>宁遁碧霄之外。己知蹇步。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376552_comment'></div>可造遥程。藉以宇内迹单。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376552_comment'></div>天涯亲老。一旦有兹殊遇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376552_comment'></div>得此吉祥。买臣何愧于负薪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376552_comment'></div>毛义实荣于捧檄。感深唯泣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376552_comment'></div>喜极翻惊。沥胆隳肝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376552_comment'></div>空寓郑庄之驿。糜躯碎首。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376552_comment'></div>何裨元礼之门。攀谢兢惶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376552_comment'></div>罔知所措。下情无任战越悚惕屏营之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376552_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_77_1376552_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=874&endYear=874')">874年6月</a>　应广州州试得举、后入长安应进士第，有文。作品：《 段先辈启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span>《 第二启》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376566' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376566' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376566?labeling=true' target='_blank'>段先辈启</a><span class='authorDate'>（874年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376566")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376566_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376566'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376566'>判官先辈万顷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376566", 1376566, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>襟神</span>。四科文行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376566_comment'></div>比鸾鹤而既冲霄汉。喻龟龙而须瑞皇王。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376566_comment'></div>今者宾幕清风。士林重价。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376566_comment'></div>虽欲留欢于五辟。其如积望于九迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376566_comment'></div>伏计即有新荣。别膺殊命。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376566_comment'></div>滔蒙知既异。感德常深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376566_comment'></div>辞违遽变于暄寒。祷祝敢忘于朝夕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376566_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1376566_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

成都

福建

href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47414")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47414_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47414'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47414'>老归江上村，孤寂欲何言。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47414'>世乱时人物，家贫后子孙。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47414'>青山寒带雨，古木夜啼猿。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47414'>惆怅西川举，戎装度剑门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47414'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47414_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_47414'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(47414)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><div id='poem_47504' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47504' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47504?labeling=true' target='_blank'>壬癸岁书情</a><span class='authorDate'>（883年8月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47504")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_47504_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47504'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47504'>故园招隐客，应便笑无成。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47504'>谒帝逢移国，投文值用兵。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47504'>孤松怜鹤在，疏柳恶蝉鸣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47504'>匹马迷归处，青云失曩情。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47504'>江头寒夜宿，垄上<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_47504", 47504, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>歉年</span>耕。<div id='poem_sentence_4_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_47504'>冠盖新人物，渔樵旧弟兄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_47504'>易生唯白发，难立是浮名。<div id='poem_sentence_6_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_47504'>惆怅灞桥路，秋风谁入行。<div id='poem_sentence_7_47504_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_47504'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_47504_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

id='poem_sentence_0_47334'>师名自越彻秦中，秦越难寻师所从。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47334_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47334'>墨迹两般诗一首，香炉峰下似相逢。<div 安陆

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=891&endYear=891')">891年</a>　入京应举经安州，有诗念郑郑諴。作品：《经安州感故郑郎中二首》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_47400' class='_poem'><div -----title
泉州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='768ff009ee624829bf29b4e1e8517df2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("768ff009ee624829bf29b4e1e8517df2");'><span id='768ff009ee624829bf29b4e1e8517df2_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=895&endYear=895')">895年</a>　南归至福建，感少时生活，至华严寺，有文。作品：《华严寺开山始祖碑铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376600' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376600' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376600?labeling=true' target='_blank'>华严寺开山始祖碑铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（895年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376600")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376600_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376600'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376600'>师法号行标。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376600_comment'></div>俗姓方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376600_comment'></div>祖荣父安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376600_comment'></div>莆之盛族也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376600_comment'></div>师生于建中二年辛酉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376600_comment'></div>龆龀即颖悟异于诸童。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376600_comment'></div>九岁投玉涧寺<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_1376600", 1376600, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>监寺</span>神皎出家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376600_comment'></div>将二年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376600_comment'></div>嘉其拔萃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376600_comment'></div>命之落发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376600_comment'></div>师以梵行未至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376600_comment'></div>不敢预大僧数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376600_comment'></div>至贞元十七年<span class='inlineComment2'>（时师年二十一）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376600_comment'></div>方薙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1376600", 1376600, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>鬓髭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376600_comment'></div>翼日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376600_comment'></div>遽讲所习涅槃经。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376600_comment'></div>一寺叹服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376600_comment'></div>既而辞其师北游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376600_comment'></div>抵京荐福寺受戒品。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376600_comment'></div>诣章教大师法会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376600_comment'></div>章教奇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376600_comment'></div>令首其众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376600_comment'></div>凡十年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376600_comment'></div>士君子之造者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376600_comment'></div>无不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_24_1376600", 1376600, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>耸慕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376600_comment'></div>寻为功德使推入道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376600_comment'></div>宪宗善之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376600_comment'></div>元和十一年<span class='inlineComment2'>（丙申师年三十六）</span>东归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376600_comment'></div>复于玉涧焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376600_comment'></div>法雨随车。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376600_comment'></div>慈云被物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376600_comment'></div>洎武皇帝<span class='inlineComment2'>（会昌元年辛酉）</span>除佛舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376600_comment'></div>籍释子于户部。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376600_comment'></div>师则巾华阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376600_comment'></div>衣缝掖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376600_comment'></div>晦迹樵客。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376600_comment'></div>庐于西岩石室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376600_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_37_1376600", 1376600, "Clauses/37/Comments/0")'>律身</span>守道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376600_comment'></div>如居千众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376600_comment'></div>及宣皇帝复寺<span class='inlineComment2'>（大中元年丁卯师年六十七）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376600_comment'></div>剌史琅琊王公迎以幡花。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376600_comment'></div>舍于郡开元寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376600_comment'></div>俾为<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_42_1376600", 1376600, "Clauses/42/Comments/0")'>监领</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376600_comment'></div>大中六年<span id='poem_sentence_45_1376600_comment'></div>乞归故山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376600_comment'></div>先时玉涧之北岩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376600_comment'></div>泉石之奇也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376600_comment'></div>卜而居之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376600_comment'></div>县令中山甄宿与莆之士庶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376600_comment'></div>争沐醍醐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376600_comment'></div>共隆兰若。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376600_comment'></div>烟峦蔽亏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376600_comment'></div>朱碧掩映。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376600_comment'></div>前俯平川。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376600_comment'></div>言未尝及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376600_comment'></div>而人知其博古也。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376600_comment'></div>所至清风凛凛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376600_comment'></div>政所谓释子之高杰者也。<div class='inline' class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376600_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_101_1376600", 1376600, "Clauses/101/Comments/0")'>胶掌</span>而拜影堂。<div
