ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=897&endYear=897')">897年</a>，58岁</div><div id='abdbb08391ea414f9a6a68b9d2905f7e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=897&endYear=897')">897年11月</a>　居家。作品：《泉州开元寺佛殿碑记》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376594' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376594' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376594?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泉州开元寺佛殿碑记</a><span class='authorDate'>（897年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376594")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376594_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376594'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376594'>混沌死而天地生。道德销而仁义作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376594_comment'></div>情车业网。始脉旋波。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376594_comment'></div>天谓洛龟河龙。文有生而不文无生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376594_comment'></div>乃产<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_3_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/6/Comments/0")'>金圣人</span>于西国。钻智慧火。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376594_comment'></div>乾<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/8/Comments/0")'>烦恼海</span>。理不<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/9/Comments/0")'>吾吾</span>而一贯生生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376594_comment'></div>其姿电㸌于周室。其波派漾于汉代。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376594_comment'></div>繇是馆移鸿胪。城崇白马。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376594_comment'></div>斯有寺之始也。寺制殿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376594_comment'></div>象王者之居。尊其法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376594_comment'></div>其后金地莲扃。周旋四海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376594_comment'></div>乌飞兔走。或故或新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376594_comment'></div>至如神运之灵莫灵矣。亦靡得而岿然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376594_comment'></div>则我州开元寺佛殿之与经楼钟楼。一夕飞烬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376594_comment'></div>斯革故鼎新之数也。初仆射太原公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376594_comment'></div>以子房之帷幄布泉城。以叔度之<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_14_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/29/Comments/0")'>裤襦</span>纩泉民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376594_comment'></div>而谓<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/30/Comments/0")'>竺乾</span>之道与<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/30/Comments/1")'>尼聃</span>鼎。宜根乎信而友乎理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376594_comment'></div>矧开元受宇。五十载之圣容。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376594_comment'></div>实寺之冠。洎帅闽也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376594_comment'></div>愈进其诚。缮经三千卷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376594_comment'></div>皆极<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_19_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/38/Comments/0")'>越藤</span>之精。书工之妙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376594_comment'></div>驾以白马十乘。送以府僧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376594_comment'></div>迎以郡僧。置兹之楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376594_comment'></div>既而□□□□蜀雨不飞。识者以为物之尤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376594_comment'></div>罕留于世。敬之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376594_comment'></div>必动乎神。是必为地祗所搜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376594_comment'></div>龙宫之索。不然者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376594_comment'></div>曷与斯故新之数期。厥理则明。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376594_comment'></div>我宜悄然不已。仲弟检校工部尚书为兹郡之秋也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376594_comment'></div>武则拍孙吴之背。文则席夏商于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376594_comment'></div>而复龙虎之内。以埙以篪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376594_comment'></div>大耸孟龙之旨。乃割俸三千缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376594_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/62/Comments/0")'>鸠工</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/62/Comments/1")'>度木</span>。烟岩<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_31_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/63/Comments/0")'>云谷</span>之杞梓楩楠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376594_comment'></div>投刃以时。趋功以隙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376594_comment'></div>食以月粟。付以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/67/Comments/0")'>心倕</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376594_comment'></div>不期年而宝殿涌出。栋隆旧绮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376594_comment'></div>梁修新虹。八表四隅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376594_comment'></div>悉半文丈。柱盛镜础。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376594_comment'></div>方圭丛斗。楣承蟠螭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376594_comment'></div>飞云翼栱。文榱刻桷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376594_comment'></div>轇轕𭩚枒。或经纬以开织。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376594_comment'></div>或丹雘而缬耀。皛若螭窟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376594_comment'></div>嶪如鳌背。风夏触而秋生。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376594_comment'></div>僧朝梵而谷应。升者骨冰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376594_comment'></div>观者<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_43_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/86/Comments/0")'>目波</span>。而五间两厦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376594_comment'></div>昔之制也。自东迦叶佛释迦牟尼佛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376594_comment'></div>左右真容。次弥勒佛弥陀佛阿难迦叶菩萨卫神。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376594_comment'></div>虽法程有常。而相貌之欲动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376594_comment'></div>东北隅则揭钟楼。其钟也新铸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376594_comment'></div>仍伟旧规。西北隅则揭经楼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376594_comment'></div>双立岳峰。两危<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_49_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>蜃云</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376594_comment'></div>东瞰全城。西吞半郭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376594_comment'></div>霜韵扣而江山四爽。金字骈而讲诵千来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376594_comment'></div>是知天地日月。鬼神不欲一存其物。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376594_comment'></div>将有待于后人也。设使斯殿也斯楼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376594_comment'></div>不有之故。其何以新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376594_comment'></div>我公之作之为。其何以布之哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376594_comment'></div>三略六韬。流通贝多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376594_comment'></div>戈霜剑雪。为甘露洁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376594_comment'></div>信英智之所措也。既毕召化内之缁锡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376594_comment'></div>数迈于千斋而落之。其中慈云五色。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376594_comment'></div>慧日重轮。谭者以为梵天之宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376594_comment'></div>化于是矣。灵山之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376594_comment'></div>俨于是矣。我公之倅试大理评事宋君曰骈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376594_comment'></div>才推博古。识洞真如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376594_comment'></div>请立贞珉。垂于不朽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376594_comment'></div>公以小儒不佞。俾刻斯文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376594_comment'></div>僧正临坛大德僧宣一。桑门之关楗者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376594_comment'></div>曰。寺有记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376594_comment'></div>亡之矣。垂拱三年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376594_comment'></div>郡儒黄守恭宅桑树吐白莲花。舍为莲花道场。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376594_comment'></div>后三年。升为兴教寺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376594_comment'></div>复为龙兴寺。逮玄宗之流圣仪也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376594_comment'></div>卜胜无以甲兹。遂为开元寺焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376594_comment'></div>尝有紫云覆寺至地。至今凡草不生其庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376594_comment'></div>大矣哉。自垂拱之迄开元。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376594_comment'></div>四朝而四易号及<span class='inlineComment2'>（句）</span>。谅兆水于木。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376594_comment'></div>垂云薙草<span class='inlineComment2'>（谓桑莲之与云草）</span>。天启地灵之如是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376594_comment'></div>则开元实寺之冠。斯又冠开元焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376594_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_78_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>金圣人</span>无为也。尧舜亦无为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376594_comment'></div>诚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1376594", 1376594, "Clauses/158/Comments/0")'>参错</span>其道。巍巍圣仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376594_comment'></div>永与诸佛如来俱。岂不其然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376594_comment'></div>愚是以奋笔于一公之说。乾宁四年丁巳冬十一月日记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376594_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_82_1376594_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='aaed3f9ec6bf4f7aa00ec60e82c15a61_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("aaed3f9ec6bf4f7aa00ec60e82c15a61");'><span id='aaed3f9ec6bf4f7aa00ec60e82c15a61_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=901')">900-901年</a>，61-62岁</div><div id='aaed3f9ec6bf4f7aa00ec60e82c15a61' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=900')">900年1月15日</a>　归闽，撰文祭祀好友陈峤。作品：《祭陈侍御峤》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376603' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376603' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376603?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭陈侍御<span class='inlineComment2'>（峤）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（900年1月15日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376603")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376603_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376603'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376603'>维光化三年岁次庚申正月庚寅朔十五日甲辰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376603_comment'></div>将仕郎守国子四门博士黄滔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376603_comment'></div>谨以清酌之奠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376603_comment'></div>敬祭于侍御陈君延封之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376603_comment'></div>伏以灵闽之江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376603_comment'></div>莆称秀绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376603_comment'></div>首武德之科级。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376603_comment'></div>自贞元之英哲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376603_comment'></div>其后继生硕儒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376603_comment'></div>亹亹鸿都。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376603_comment'></div>交怀荆璞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376603_comment'></div>互握隋珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376603_comment'></div>皆指期于拾芥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376603_comment'></div>终恸哭于弯弧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376603_comment'></div>洎宣皇之后年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376603_comment'></div>则夫子之斯出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376603_comment'></div>持曾参之孝行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376603_comment'></div>袖孟轲之文帙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376603_comment'></div>荐赋诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376603_comment'></div>上书圣日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376603_comment'></div>射宫而劲挺弦矢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376603_comment'></div>艺圃而葳蕤华实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376603_comment'></div>难亨者吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376603_comment'></div>难偶者至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376603_comment'></div>管仲三奔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376603_comment'></div>非战之过。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376603_comment'></div>孙宏十上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376603_comment'></div>盖时未通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376603_comment'></div>七千里而辛勤上国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376603_comment'></div>二十年而惆怅东风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376603_comment'></div>人皆一一以兴愤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376603_comment'></div>我独孜孜而养蒙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376603_comment'></div>既而凤阙飞尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376603_comment'></div>龟城挂榜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376603_comment'></div>仪曹方急于中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376603_comment'></div>权宦辄窥其上赏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376603_comment'></div>殊不知杨吟诵于犬子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376603_comment'></div>景荐延乎商鞅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376603_comment'></div>古为不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376603_comment'></div>吾肯斯仿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376603_comment'></div>谁不奇夫子之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376603_comment'></div>谁不高夫子之名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376603_comment'></div>冰霜却污。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376603_comment'></div>松柏居贞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376603_comment'></div>渭水之钓有守。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376603_comment'></div>武城之径宁行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376603_comment'></div>逮夫岷峨岁改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376603_comment'></div>岐雍烟清。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376603_comment'></div>天子复含元谒见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376603_comment'></div>有司新都省权衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376603_comment'></div>巍巍令闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376603_comment'></div>赫赫嘉声。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376603_comment'></div>遂从寰海。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376603_comment'></div>回翥蓬瀛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376603_comment'></div>振辉光于甲乙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376603_comment'></div>开道路于孤平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376603_comment'></div>望高而先脱麻衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376603_comment'></div>家远而须荣乡土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376603_comment'></div>十二人林君茂躅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376603_comment'></div>一百年莆邑大数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376603_comment'></div>君侯<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_60_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/60/Comments/0")'>设醴</span>以前席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376603_comment'></div>里巷<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_61_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/61/Comments/0")'>拜尘</span>而如堵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376603_comment'></div>雷车轞轞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376603_comment'></div>鹤贺翩翩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376603_comment'></div>初命就门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376603_comment'></div>见东周之三语。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376603_comment'></div>前程不日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376603_comment'></div>候西汉之七迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376603_comment'></div>旋以孔樽引满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376603_comment'></div>徐榻解悬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376603_comment'></div>白璧黄金而謺矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376603_comment'></div>玳簪珠履以加焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376603_comment'></div>列藩所得者贤才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376603_comment'></div>古人所重者知己。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376603_comment'></div>既将推珍于席上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376603_comment'></div>岂独矜词于雪里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376603_comment'></div>庄周说剑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376603_comment'></div>则韩魏呈镡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376603_comment'></div>郭隗升台。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376603_comment'></div>则<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_79_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/79/Comments/0")'>乐邹</span>觏止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376603_comment'></div>绣衣曜日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376603_comment'></div>骢马嘶烟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376603_comment'></div>飞诏而宾阶次第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376603_comment'></div>假途而寺盘旋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376603_comment'></div>莫不汉帷驻策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376603_comment'></div>薛石留笺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376603_comment'></div>从容渥泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376603_comment'></div>宠异<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_87_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/87/Comments/0")'>淹延</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376603_comment'></div>胡言薤露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376603_comment'></div>忽败椿年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376603_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376603_comment'></div>石火风烛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376603_comment'></div>惊波逝川。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376603_comment'></div>圣贤之不免矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376603_comment'></div>古今之共痛焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376603_comment'></div>滔江乡则中外亲姻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376603_comment'></div>帝里则参差<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_96_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/96/Comments/0")'>砚席</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376603_comment'></div>干名而后乎一纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376603_comment'></div>论友而仰乎三益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376603_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_99_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>蝉槐</span>给念。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376603_comment'></div>几同京洛之愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376603_comment'></div>莺柳看时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376603_comment'></div>各署神仙之籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376603_comment'></div>别来辇下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376603_comment'></div>归自瓯中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376603_comment'></div>尘忝而郤诜<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_105_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/105/Comments/0")'>桂绿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376603_comment'></div>因依而王俭莲红。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376603_comment'></div>断金益固。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376603_comment'></div>投漆攸同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376603_comment'></div>见行藏于柱史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376603_comment'></div>论倚伏于塞翁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376603_comment'></div>实期以始者文场之懿德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376603_comment'></div>迩来使府之清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376603_comment'></div>伏蒲北省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376603_comment'></div>起草南宫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376603_comment'></div>更雪当时之冤滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376603_comment'></div>少为吾党之隆崇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376603_comment'></div>是何天之丧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376603_comment'></div>道之穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376603_comment'></div>悤悤大夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376603_comment'></div>默默元穹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376603_comment'></div>滔复晓夕以思。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376603_comment'></div>江山之事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376603_comment'></div>林君则以合浦垂名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376603_comment'></div>夫子则以申秦得意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376603_comment'></div>高步斯振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376603_comment'></div>宏规靡异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1376603_comment'></div>前辈旷世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1376603_comment'></div>后来遂志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1376603_comment'></div>俱蟠使下之柏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1376603_comment'></div>俱擅乙中之二<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1376603_comment'></div>推是言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1376603_comment'></div>岂偶然耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1376603_comment'></div>贤哲相望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1376603_comment'></div>今昔一致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1376603_comment'></div>呜呼延封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1376603_comment'></div>昨日而冰壶仙雾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1376603_comment'></div>今辰而丹旐刍灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1376603_comment'></div>虽死生之理能一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1376603_comment'></div>终痛伤之恳罔宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1376603_comment'></div>况以平生树德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1376603_comment'></div>幽宅刊铭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1376603_comment'></div>无惭郭泰之贤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1376603_comment'></div>笺毫曷措。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1376603_comment'></div>爰枉赵岐之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1376603_comment'></div>涕泪交零。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1376603_comment'></div>水咽云愁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1376603_comment'></div>风悲日暮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1376603_comment'></div>精灵一闭于泉壤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1376603_comment'></div>岁月空苍于垄树。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1376603_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_150_1376603", 1376603, "Clauses/150/Comments/0")'>椒壶</span>略备。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1376603_comment'></div>兰俎聊具。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1376603_comment'></div>申永诀于斯言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1376603_comment'></div>庶冥感其诚素。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1376603_comment'></div>呜呼哀哉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_154_1376603_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1376603'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_130_1376603_0'>⑴ 林端公贞元七年首闽越之科第以珠还合浦赋擅名后十年莆邑许员外荣登自此文学之士继踵而悉不偶时旷八十七年始钟于延封其文以申秦续篇擅名后六七年徐正字及第兼滔尘忝林端公同延封榜皆第十二人皆开路于后人皆终使府大判官判官皆柏台林荆南延封闽中也</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1376603_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=900')">900年1月17日</a>　为陈峤撰墓志铭。作品：《司直陈公墓志铭》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376602' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376602' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376602?labeling=true' target='_blank'>司直陈公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（900年1月17日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376602")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376602_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376602'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376602'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>姬孔</span>之教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376602_comment'></div>与日月以悬天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376602_comment'></div>颜闵之馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376602_comment'></div>作芝兰而出地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376602_comment'></div>可不诔清尘于桂苑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376602_comment'></div>揭贞石于<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>松阡</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376602_comment'></div>叙白杨之别生悲风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376602_comment'></div>示黄壤之下藏嘉气者哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376602_comment'></div>汉太邱长二十三世孙南安县尉讳真。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376602_comment'></div>生处士荛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376602_comment'></div>荛生大理评事齐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376602_comment'></div>忠信笃敬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376602_comment'></div>不类今世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376602_comment'></div>尝有白雀巢其庭宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376602_comment'></div>佳莲产其池塘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376602_comment'></div>识者谓其后必大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376602_comment'></div>有子九人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376602_comment'></div>皆力儒学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376602_comment'></div>公其长也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376602_comment'></div>讳峤字延封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376602_comment'></div>龆龀好学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376602_comment'></div>弱冠能文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376602_comment'></div>与高阳许龟图江夏黄彦修居莆之北岩精舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376602_comment'></div>五年而二子西去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376602_comment'></div>复居北平山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376602_comment'></div>两地穴管宁之榻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376602_comment'></div>十霜索随氏之珠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376602_comment'></div>然后应诏诸侯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376602_comment'></div>求试宗伯。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376602_comment'></div>而以咸通乾符之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376602_comment'></div>龙门有万仞之险。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376602_comment'></div>莺谷无孤飞之羽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376602_comment'></div>才名则温歧韩铢罗隐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376602_comment'></div>皆<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_33_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/33/Comments/0")'>退黜</span>不已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376602_comment'></div>故公自丁丑之及丙申。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376602_comment'></div>高价驰而逸步踬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376602_comment'></div>既而大盗移国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376602_comment'></div>德公文行之深者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376602_comment'></div>安州郑郎中諴孙拾遗泰叹而勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376602_comment'></div>久乃持辇下之屈名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376602_comment'></div>适蜀中之贡府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376602_comment'></div>致卿士倒屣场席。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376602_comment'></div>开路清风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376602_comment'></div>既而窃为权官沽诸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376602_comment'></div>将求识而荐之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376602_comment'></div>公时己出经试。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376602_comment'></div>比言之者□荣纸而亡是举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376602_comment'></div>光启二年收开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376602_comment'></div>三年荣登故相荥阳郑公礼部上第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376602_comment'></div>大哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376602_comment'></div>公为人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_50_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/50/Comments/0")'>谨信</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376602_comment'></div>居家纯孝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376602_comment'></div>事继亲弥善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376602_comment'></div>庐先君墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376602_comment'></div>泣血有闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376602_comment'></div>其所为文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376602_comment'></div>扣孟轲扬雄户牖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376602_comment'></div>凡三百篇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376602_comment'></div>有表奏牍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376602_comment'></div>颇为前辈推工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376602_comment'></div>且大唐之设网士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376602_comment'></div>得之于是者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376602_comment'></div>岁几人焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376602_comment'></div>矧复有避宦者之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376602_comment'></div>若走冲虚之车焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376602_comment'></div>荥阳公自以得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376602_comment'></div>其春首门人脱麻摄京兆府参军。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376602_comment'></div>司空太原公帅闽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376602_comment'></div>解榻以礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376602_comment'></div>辟之为大从事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376602_comment'></div>受大理评事兼监察御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376602_comment'></div>今府相继拥于节旄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376602_comment'></div>益贤其<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_72_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/72/Comments/0")'>参画</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376602_comment'></div>奏大理司直兼殿中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376602_comment'></div>方期辍从藩屏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376602_comment'></div>入践谏垣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376602_comment'></div>不幸寝疾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376602_comment'></div>浃辰<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_77_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/77/Comments/0")'>不起</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376602_comment'></div>享龄七十有五。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376602_comment'></div>光化二年十月三日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376602_comment'></div>呜呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376602_comment'></div>将来失其龟镜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376602_comment'></div>斲者丧其般倕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376602_comment'></div>虽登大年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376602_comment'></div>终恨朝露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376602_comment'></div>三年庚申正月十七日丙午。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376602_comment'></div>葬于泉州莆田县崇教里北平故山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376602_comment'></div>礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376602_comment'></div>公两娶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376602_comment'></div>鲁国林夫人荥阳潘夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376602_comment'></div>其子三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376602_comment'></div>仲曰说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376602_comment'></div>买石太湖刊文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376602_comment'></div>愚与公同邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376602_comment'></div>闽越江山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376602_comment'></div>莆阳为灵秀之最。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376602_comment'></div>贞元中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376602_comment'></div>林端公藻冠东南之科第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376602_comment'></div>十年而许员外稷继翔其后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376602_comment'></div>词人<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_99_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>亹亹</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376602_comment'></div>若陈厚庆陈泛陈黯林颢许温林速许龟图黄彦修许超林郁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376602_comment'></div>俱以梦笔之词。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376602_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_102_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/102/Comments/0")'>籯金</span>之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1376602_comment'></div>半生随计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1376602_comment'></div>没齿衔冤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1376602_comment'></div>旷乎百年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1376602_comment'></div>而公追二贤之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1376602_comment'></div>七年而徐正字寅捷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1376602_comment'></div>八年而愚□莫不以江山之数耶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1376602_comment'></div>猗欤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1376602_comment'></div>昔之负高才不以位而碑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1376602_comment'></div>襄阳惟孟先生焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1376602_comment'></div>今也累懿德不隆位而碑者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1376602_comment'></div>以陈夫子始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1376602_comment'></div>愚<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_114_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/114/Comments/0")'>沾巾</span>宿草。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1376602_comment'></div>无愧抽毫。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1376602_comment'></div>其辞曰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1376602_comment'></div>江山之秀钟乎人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1376602_comment'></div>纯孝高节并其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1376602_comment'></div>掬兹二美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1376602_comment'></div>摛为雄文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1376602_comment'></div>以之登<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_121_1376602", 1376602, "Clauses/121/Comments/0")'>桂科</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1376602_comment'></div>以之列莲宾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1376602_comment'></div>斯为君子。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1376602_comment'></div>谁曰未仁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1376602_comment'></div>呜呼九原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1376602_comment'></div>宜树贞珉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_126_1376602_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=900')">900年3月</a>　写诗贺王审邽加左仆射。作品：《贺清源仆射新命》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_47409' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_47409' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/47409?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺清源仆射新命</a><span class='authorDate'>（900年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_47409")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_47409_comment'></div><div class='titleComment' id='poem_allusion_47409'><span class='label'>引用典故：</span><span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4979, "poem_allusion_47409")'>荆树</span></div><div id='poem_allusion_47409_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_47409'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_47409'>虽言嵩岳秀崔嵬，少降连枝<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_47409", 47409, "Clauses/1/Comments/0")'>命世才</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_47409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_47409'>南史两荣唯百揆，东闽双拜有三台<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_47409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_47409'>二天在顶家家咏，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_47409", 47409, "Clauses/5/Comments/0")'>丹凤</span>衔书岁岁来。<div id='poem_sentence_2_47409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_47409'>虚说古贤龙虎盛，谁攀<span class='link' onclick='ShowAllusionComment(4979, "poem_sentence_3_47409")'>荆树</span>上金台。<div id='poem_sentence_3_47409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_47409'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_47409_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_47409'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_47409_0'>⑴ 《南史》“袁宪兄弟同为仆射，当时荣之”，殊未若今清源与府城，并拜仆射，兼带台席之尊</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_47409_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=900&endYear=900')">900年11月</a>　撰文祭祀好友林用谦。作品：《祭林先辈（用谦）》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376607' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376607' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376607?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭林先辈<span class='inlineComment2'>（用谦）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（900年11月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376607")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376607_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376607'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376607'>维光化三年岁次庚申十一月日。敬祭于林君执友之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376607_comment'></div>惟灵。夫渥洼之足。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376607_comment'></div>以千里之为程。已驰之而俄沮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376607_comment'></div>嶰谷之音。以六律之为府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376607_comment'></div>既参之而忽泯。夫不永其终始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376607_comment'></div>何痛如之。呜呼林君。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376607_comment'></div>得以言矣。君负相如之词赋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376607_comment'></div>慕郤氏之科名。一纪秦城。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376607_comment'></div>千门祢剌。虽众口大馨其凤藻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376607_comment'></div>人罕如焉。而三春累困于莺乔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376607_comment'></div>数何奇也。然则女贞而十年必字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376607_comment'></div>药灵而九转须成。果契至公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376607_comment'></div>克升上第。既己东堂得意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376607_comment'></div>南国言旋。龙珠则动彩于握中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376607_comment'></div>雁字则增辉于天际。将冀盛清风于吾道。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376607_comment'></div>岂期叹逝水于人生。屈原之难问者天。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376607_comment'></div>蔡泽之不知者命。螺江烟景。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376607_comment'></div>方翻丁令之羽毛。驹隙光阴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376607_comment'></div>俄启曾参之手足。诚寿天靡移于夙契。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376607_comment'></div>且鬼神何害于善人。祸福吉凶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376607_comment'></div>悠扬暧昧。凄凉物理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376607_comment'></div>惨怛人情。今则寿域斯开。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376607_comment'></div>贞魂永蛰。垄头水咽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376607_comment'></div>山上云愁。邓攸之继世无儿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376607_comment'></div>语留身后。崔曙之遗孤有女。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376607_comment'></div>诗在生前。虽盛衰之同休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376607_comment'></div>亦存亡之至痛。滔京关进退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376607_comment'></div>砚席参差。幸忝先鸣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376607_comment'></div>弥欣继捷。未贺桂枝之入手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376607_comment'></div>忽从薤露以伤心。脩短有兹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376607_comment'></div>吁嗟何极。灵輀戒路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376607_comment'></div>丹旐翻风。远寓丹诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376607_comment'></div>聊陈薄奠。愿垂冥感。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376607_comment'></div>鉴歆于斯。呜呼哀哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376607_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_34_1376607_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=901&endYear=901')">901年1月</a>　撰文祭陈鼎，鼎，大顺二年进士。作品：《祭陈先辈鼎》<span class='inlineComment2'>（其生年不可确考，故表中年岁是不确定的数字。）</span><div id='poem_1376606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1376606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1376606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>祭陈先辈<span class='inlineComment2'>（鼎）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（901年1月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 晚唐 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(21690, "晚唐", "黄滔", "poem_title_1376606")'>黄滔</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1376606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1376606'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1376606'>维光化四年岁次辛酉正月二十七日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1376606_comment'></div>祭于东君之灵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1376606_comment'></div>闽山秀气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1376606_comment'></div>鲁国清尘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1376606_comment'></div>天之授受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1376606_comment'></div>钟我仁人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1376606_comment'></div>卓矣生世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1376606_comment'></div>学而立身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1376606_comment'></div>卫玠则旁辉其舅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1376606_comment'></div>曾参则大孝于亲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1376606_comment'></div>始者随计归越。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1376606_comment'></div>上书入秦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1376606_comment'></div><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_1376606", 1376606, "Clauses/12/Comments/0")'>擅价</span>而侯门倾动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1376606_comment'></div>呈功而凤藻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_13_1376606", 1376606, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>精新</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1376606_comment'></div>咸通之年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1376606_comment'></div>九霄也鹢路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1376606_comment'></div>乾符之际。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1376606_comment'></div>万仞也龙津。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1376606_comment'></div>既而瓯岭经兵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1376606_comment'></div>蜀川迎帝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1376606_comment'></div>匪无随驾之恳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1376606_comment'></div>实切问安之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1376606_comment'></div>肩负<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_22_1376606", 1376606, "Clauses/22/Comments/0")'>燋饭</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1376606_comment'></div>志销丹桂。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1376606_comment'></div>虽深藏豹之诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1376606_comment'></div>难遏化鲲之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1376606_comment'></div>都堂昔日。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1376606_comment'></div>困一千辈之交锋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1376606_comment'></div>大国中兴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1376606_comment'></div>作第二人之登第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1376606_comment'></div>杏园醉后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1376606_comment'></div>华表归时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1376606_comment'></div>往岁井邑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1376606_comment'></div>兹辰羽仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1376606_comment'></div>旋属姑苏积衅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1376606_comment'></div>勾践兴师。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1376606_comment'></div>于是板舆避地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1376606_comment'></div>草檄从知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1376606_comment'></div>百越之江光汹涌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1376606_comment'></div>四明之山翠参差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1376606_comment'></div>长鲸既剔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1376606_comment'></div>逸足难羁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1376606_comment'></div>东别朱门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1376606_comment'></div>南还故里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1376606_comment'></div>一朝而奄至泣血。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1376606_comment'></div>三载而蔑闻<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1376606", 1376606, "Clauses/45/Comments/0")'>见齿</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1376606_comment'></div>仲由此后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1376606_comment'></div>千钟之禄悠哉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1376606_comment'></div>毛义终身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1376606_comment'></div>一檄之荣已矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1376606_comment'></div>修程不顾。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1376606_comment'></div>盛德逾馨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1376606_comment'></div>田园草绿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1376606_comment'></div>户牖山青。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1376606_comment'></div>与夔龙而抗迹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1376606_comment'></div>追园绮而忘形。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1376606_comment'></div>且期齐鹤算。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1376606_comment'></div>寿陟龟龄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1376606_comment'></div>是何修短之期莫测。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1376606_comment'></div>吉凶之阈难扃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1376606_comment'></div>明神罔佑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1376606_comment'></div>大祸斯丁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1376606_comment'></div>士林惨怛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1376606_comment'></div>词苑伶俜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1376606_comment'></div>滔始自童年。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1376606_comment'></div>至于壮岁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1376606_comment'></div>江乡为竹马之友。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1376606_comment'></div>京辇作谷莺之会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1376606_comment'></div>三朝被刖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1376606_comment'></div>栖迟泣荆璞之艰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1376606_comment'></div>十上遭时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1376606_comment'></div>次第到瑶蟾之内。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1376606_comment'></div>谁言倏忽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1376606_comment'></div>遽叹存亡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1376606_comment'></div>痛人琴之俱绝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1376606_comment'></div>缅胶漆以空伤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1376606_comment'></div>呜呼用新。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1376606_comment'></div>平生德行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1376606_comment'></div>曩昔文章。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1376606_comment'></div>近则孟浩然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1376606_comment'></div>虽人间不仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1376606_comment'></div>远则卜子夏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1376606_comment'></div>乃地下为郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1376606_comment'></div>诚以高科而贞退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1376606_comment'></div>固从阴骘以舒张。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1376606_comment'></div>逝水东流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1376606_comment'></div>踆乌西匿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1376606_comment'></div>昨辰而椒桂献酬。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1376606_comment'></div>今日而藻蘋滴沥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1376606_comment'></div>且彭祖之延永寿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1376606_comment'></div>亦至<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_90_1376606", 1376606, "Clauses/90/Comments/0")'>销磨</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1376606_comment'></div>而巨卿之哭故人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1376606_comment'></div>得无悽恻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1376606_comment'></div>况乎东西多故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1376606_comment'></div>南北遥程。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1376606_comment'></div>不得亲随薤露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1376606_comment'></div>送别松茔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1376606_comment'></div>既阙殷勤而执绋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1376606_comment'></div>空将呜咽以沾缨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1376606_comment'></div>谨以<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_99_1376606", 1376606, "Clauses/99/Comments/0")'>依稀</span>蔬果。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1376606_comment'></div>一二精诚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1376606_comment'></div>愿冥符于肸蚃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1376606_comment'></div>申永诀于幽明。</div><div id='poem_sentence_102_1376606_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

杭州
